vitiṇṇaparalokassa natthi pāpaṃ akāriyanti (itivu 27)
ti yo karoti tassa santāne phaluppādapaccayabhāvena uppatti evañhi natthi kammaṃ natthi kammaphalanti akiriyavādassa paripuṇṇatā sati hi kammaphale kammānamakiriyabhāvo kathaṃ bhavissati ti karototiādinā vuttena sabbappakārenapi
nti likucaṃ  na raññā puṭṭhaṃ sandiṭṭhikaṃ sāmaññaphalaṃ byākarotīti adhippāyo idañhi avadhāraṇaṃ vipākapaṭikkhepanivattanatthaṃ yo hi kammaṃ paṭikkhipati tena atthato vipākopi paṭikkhittoyeva nāma hoti tathā hi vakkhati kammaṃ paṭibāhantenāpītiādi (dī ni aṭṭha 1170-172)
paṭirājūhi anabhibhavanīyabhāvena visesato jitanti  ekassa rañño āṇāpavattideso mā mayhaṃ vijite vasathāti apasādanā pabbajitassa pabbājanasaṅkhātā viheṭhanāyevāti  vuttaṃ nti tena vuttassa atthassa evametanti upadhāraṇaṃ sallakkhaṇaṃ  tadaminā paṭikkhipatīti āha ti tassa pana atthassa addhaniyabhāvāpādanavasena cittena sandhāraṇaṃ  tadaminā paṭikkhipatīti dasseti ti iminā ti uttamavaseneva avitathattā vā parehi anuccālito thirabhūto attho apheggubhāvena sāroti vuccati taṃvasenevāti attho nti vaṭṭato niyyānaṃ ti aviparītattho uttamassa vā ñāṇassārammaṇabhūto attho  tathāyeva bhagavato santike bhāsitattā

ti hetupaccayapaṭisedhavacanena ti iminā sabhāvato vijjamānasseva paṭikkhipane tassa aññāṇameva kāraṇanti dasseti nti saṃkilissanassa malīnassa kāraṇaṃ  nti saṃkilesato visuddhiyā vodānassa paccayaṃ ti paccattavacanassa e-kāravasena padasiddhi yathā vanappagumbe yathā phusitaggeti (khu pā 13 su ni 236) paccattatthe vā bhummavacanaṃ yathā idampissa hoti sīlasminti (dī ni 1194) tadevatthaṃ dasseti ti iminā so ca tena tena sattena attanā kātabbakammaṃ attanā nipphādetabbapayogo vā tenāha tiādi nti sammāsambodhiṃ nti attanā katakammaṃ ti natthi parakāreti padena  parassa vāhasā ijjhanakapayogo tena vuttaṃ ntiādi nti ovādabhūtamanusāsaniṃ paṭhamaṃ vā ovādo pacchā anusāsanī parakāranti padassa upalakkhaṇavasena atthadassanañcetaṃ lokuttaradhamme parakārāvassayo natthīti āha nti atthevesa lokiyadhamme yathā taṃ amhākaṃ bodhisattassa āḷārudake nissāya pañcābhiññālokiyasamāpattilābho tañca pacchimabhavikamahāsattaṃ sandhāya vuttaṃ paccekabodhisattassapi ettheva saṅgaho tesampi tadabhāvato nti manussesu subhagabhāvaṃ nti vuttappakārena kammavādassa kiriyavādassa ca paṭikkhipanena ti atthi bhikkhave kammaṃ kaṇhaṃ kaṇhavipākantiādi (a ni 4232) nayappavatte kammānaṃ kammaphalānañca atthitāparidīpane buddhasāsane paccanīkakathanaṃ pahāradānasadisanti ti
yathāvuttaattakāraparakārābhāvato  eva sattānaṃ paccattapurisakāro nāma koci natthīti sandhāya ti tassa paṭikkhipanaṃ dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ devattampītiādinā manussasobhagyatantiādinā ca  bale patiṭṭhitāti vatvā vīriyamevidha balanti dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ sattānañhi diṭṭhadhammikasamparāyika nibbānasampattiāvahaṃ vīriyabalaṃ natthīti so paṭikkhipati nidassanamattañcetaṃ vodāniyabalassa paṭikkhipanaṃ saṃkilesikassāpi balassa tena paṭikkhipanato yadi vīriyādīni purisakāravevacanāni atha kasmā tesaṃ visuṃ gahaṇanti āha tiādi ti idaṃ phalaṃ amhākaṃ vīriyena pavattaṃ ti aññesaṃ pavattavohāravacanassa paṭikkhepakaraṇavasena  vīriyathāmaparakkamasambandhanena pavattabalavādīnaṃ vādassa paṭikkhepakaraṇavasena natthi balanti padamiva sabbānipetāni tena ādīyantīti adhippāyo tañca vacanīyatthato vuttaṃ vacanatthato pana tassā tassā kiriyāya ussannaṭṭhena  sūravīrabhāvāvahaṭṭhena  tadeva daḷhabhāvato porisadhuraṃ vahantena pavattetabbato ca  paraṃ paraṃ ṭhānaṃ akkamanavasena pavattiyā ti veditabbaṃ
rūpādīsu sattavisattatāya  assasanapassasanavasena pavattiyā pāṇanato ti iminā atthena samānepi padadvaye ekindriyādivasena pāṇe vibhajitvā sattato visesaṃ katvā esa vadatīti āha tiādi bhavantīti ti sattapāṇapariyāyepi sati aṇḍakosādīsu sambhavanaṭṭhena tato visesāva tena vuttāti dasseti ti iminā  gabbhāsayo jīvanato pāṇaṃ dhārento viya vaḍḍhanato  tenāha tiādi saddena viruḷhadhammā tiṇarukkhā gahitā natthi etesaṃ saṃkilesavisuddhīsu vaso sāmatthiyanti  tathā  tenāha ntiādi ti niyamanā achejjasuttāvutassa abhejjamaṇino viya niyatappavattitāya gatijātibandhāpavaggavasena niyāmoti attho ti tāsu tāsu jātīsu  sambandhībhūtānaṃ  samavāyena samāgamo sambandhīnirapekkhopi bhāvasaddo sambandhīsahito viya pakatiyatthavācakoti āha ti yathā kaṇṭakassa tikkhatā kapitthaphalādīnaṃ parimaṇḍalatā migapakkhīnaṃ vicittākāratā ca evaṃ sabbassāpi lokassa hetupaccayamantarena tathā tathā pariṇāmo akuttimo sabhāvoyevāti attho tena vuttaṃ tiādi pariṇamanaṃ nānappakāratāpatti ti sattapāṇādinā yathā bhavitabbaṃ tathevāti sambandho
chaḷabhijātiyo  parato vitthārīyissanti sukhañca dukkhañca paṭisaṃvedentīti vadanto makkhali adukkhamasukhabhūmiṃ sabbena sabbaṃ na jānātīti vuttaṃ ti ayaṃ sukhañca dukkhañca paṭisaṃvedentīti  vacanaṃ karaṇabhāvena gahetvā vuttā ācariyassa mati potthakesu pana ti ayameva pāṭho diṭṭho na adukkhamasukhabhūmīti evaṃ sati chasvevābhijātīsūti vacanaṃ adhikaraṇabhāvena gahetvā chasu eva abhijātīsu sukhadukkhapaṭisaṃvedanaṃ na tehi aññattha tāyeva sukhadukkhabhūmi na tadaññāti dassetīti vuttanti veditabbaṃ ayameva ca yuttataro paṭikkhepitabbassa atthassa bhūmivasena vuttattā yadi hi sukhañca dukkhañca paṭisaṃvedentīti vacanena paṭikkhepitabbassa dassanaṃ siyā atha aññā adukkhamasukhā natthīti dasseyya na adukkhamasukhabhūmīti dassanahetuvacanassa bhūmiatthābhāvato dasseti cetaṃ tāsaṃ bhūmiyā abhāvameva tena viññāyati ayaṃ pāṭho ayañcattho yuttataroti
nti manussesu khattiyabrāhmaṇādivasena tiracchānādīsu sīhabyagghādivasena padhānayonīnaṃ padhānatā cettha uttamatā tenāha nti ti cha sahassāni pañca ca kammuno satānīti padassa atthadassanaṃ ti ti iminā kevalaṃ takkamattakena niratthakaṃ diṭṭhiṃ dīpetīti imamevatthamatidisati ettha ca ti vadanto yasmā takkikā avassayabhūtatathatthaggahaṇaaṅkusanayamantarena niraṅkusatāya parikappanassa yaṃ kiñci attanā parikappitaṃ sārato maññamānā tatheva abhinivissa tattha ca diṭṭhigāhaṃ gaṇhanti tasmā na tesaṃ diṭṭhivatthusmiṃ viññūhi vicāraṇā kātabbāti imamadhippāyaṃ vibhāveti ti uttaravihāravāsino ti cakkhādipañcindriyavasena te hi cakkhusotaghānajivhākāyasaṅkhātāni imāni pañcindriyāni pañca kammānīti titthiyā paññapentīti vadanti kāyavacīmanokammāni ca tīṇi kammānīti ti tadubhayaṃ oḷārikattā paripuṇṇakammanti laddhi manokammaṃ anoḷārikattā upaḍḍhakammanti laddhīti yojanā dvāsaṭṭhi paṭipadāti vattabbe sabhāvaniruttiṃ ajānanto dvaṭṭhipaṭipadāti vadatīti āha ti saddaracakā pana dvāsaṭṭhiyā salopo attamāti vadanti tadayuttameva sabhāvaniruttiyā yogato asiddhattā  yadi hi sā yogena siddhā assa evaṃ sabhāvaniruttiyeva siyā tathā ca sati ācariyānaṃ matena virujjhatīti vadanti cullāsīti sahassānītiādikā pana aññatra diṭṭhapayogā sabhāvaniruttiyeva dissati hi 
cullāsīti  sahassāni kappā tiṭṭhanti ye marū
na tveva tepi tiṭṭhanti dvīhi cittehi samohitāti (visuddhi 2715 mahāni 10 39)
ti catunnamasaṅkhyeyyakappānaṃ aññatarabhūte ekasmiṃ asaṅkhyeyyakappe tatthāpi ca vivaṭṭaṭṭhāyīsaññitaṃ ekameva sandhāya ti vuttaṃ na hi so assutasāsanadhammo itare jānāti bāhirakānamavisayattā ajānanto evamāhāti attho
urabbhe hananti hantvā vā jīvitaṃ kappentīti  esa nayo dīsupi ti vuttāvasesakā ye keci cātuppadajīvikā nesādā māgavikapadasmiñhi rohitādimigajātiyeva gahitā bandhanāgāre niyojentīti ti dāruṇakammantā  sabbopi kaṇhakammapasutatāya  kaṇhassa dhammassa abhijāti abbhuppatti yassāti katvā ti buddhasāsane bhikkhū ti chandarāge saññogavasena tesaṃ pakkhipanaṃ kaṇṭakasadisachandarāgena saññuttā bhuñjantīti hi adhippāyena ti vuttaṃ kasmāti ce yasmā te paṇītapaṇīte paccaye paṭisevantīti tassa micchāgāho tasmā ñāyaladdhepi paccaye bhuñjamānā ājīvakasamayassa vilomagāhitāya paccayesu kaṇṭake pakkhipitvā khādanti nāmāti vadati ti kaṇṭakena yathāvuttena saha jīvikā ti ayaṃ makkhalissa vādadīpanā attanā racitā pāḷiyevāti yathāvuttamatthaṃ samattheti kaṇṭakavuttikā eva nāma  apare  bāhirakā santi te nīlābhijātīti ti attho te hi savisesaṃ attakilamathānuyogamanuyuttā tathā hi te kaṇṭake vattantā viya bhavantīti ti vuttā nīlassa dhammassa abhijāti yassāti  evamitaresupi
amhākaṃ  saññojanagaṇṭho natthīti vādino bāhirakapabbajitā  ekameva sāṭakaṃ paridahantā  kaṇhato parisuddho nīlo tato pana lohitotiādinā yathākkamaṃ tassa parisuddhaṃ vādaṃ dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ ti bhuñjananahānapaṭikkhepādivatasamāyogena parisuddhatarā kaṇhanīlamupādāya lohitassāpi parisuddhabhāvena vattabbato ti odātavatthaparidahanā ti ājīvakasāvakabhūtā  ājīvakaladdhiyā visuddhacittatāya nigaṇṭhehipi  haliddābhānampi  purime upādāya parisuddhabhāvappattito ntiādinā tassa chandāgamanaṃ dasseti nandādīnaṃ sāvakabhūtā pabbajitā  tathā  nandādayo kira tathārūpaṃ ājīvakapaṭipattiṃ ukkaṃsaṃ pāpetvā ṭhitā tasmā nigaṇṭhehi ājīvakasāvakehi pabbajitehi paṇḍaratarā vuttā paramasukkābhijātīti ayaṃ tassa laddhi
ti padhānaniddeso itthīnampi hetā bhūmiyo esa icchateva ti accantasaññogavacanaṃ ettakampi mandā momūhāti ti mātukucchiṃ sandhāyāha  tamanussaritvā khedanaṃ kīḷanañca khiḍḍāsaddeneva saṅgahetvā  vuttā padassa nikkhipanaṃ  yadā tathā padaṃ nikkhipituṃ samattho tadā ti bhāvo vatāvatassa tiādipi tesaṃ bāhirakānaṃ pāḷiyeva tattha ti bhikkhāya vicaraṇako tesaṃ vā paṭipattiyā paṭipannako ti jiṇṇo jarāvasena hīnadhātuko attano vā paṭipattiyā paṭipakkhaṃ jinitvā ṭhito so kira tathābhūto dhammampi kassaci na kathesi tenāha ti oṭṭhavadanādivippakāre katepi khamanavasena na kiñci kathetītipi vadanti nti so na kumbhimukhā paṭiggaṇhātītiādinā nayena mahāsīhanādasutte (dī ni 1394 ma ni 1155) vuttaalābhahetusamāyogena alābhiṃ tatoyeva jighacchādubbalaparetatāya sayanaparāyanaṭṭhena 
ti sattānamājīvabhūtāni jīvikāvuttisatāni paribbājakasatānīti vuccamānepi cesa sabhāvaliṅgamajānanto ti  vadati evamaññesupi tenāha ti nāgabhavanaṃ  yathā mahiṃsakamaṇḍalanti paramāṇuādi ggahaṇena eḷakajāti gahitā ggahaṇena rurugavayādi migajāti ti phaḷumhi pabbeti attho cātumahārājikādibrahmakāyikādivasena tesañca antarabhedavasena  tattha cātumahārājikānaṃ ekaccaantarabhedo  (dī ni 2331) dīpetabbo tiādinā ajānanto panesa bahū devepi satta eva vadatīti tassa appamāṇataṃ dasseti ti dīpadesakulavaṃsājīvādivibhāgavasena pisācā eva  te aparapetādivasena  bahutarāti attho bāhirakasamaye pana chaddantadahamandākiniyo kuvāḷiyamucalindanāmena voharitāti (dī ni ṭī 1168) ācariyena vuttaṃ
ti  pabbagaṇṭhikā pabbagaṇṭhimhi hi pavuṭasaddo ti mahātaṭā pārisesanayena  evaṃ supinesupi ti idaṃ mahākappānanti atthato veditabbaṃ saddato panesa ajānanto evaṃ vadatīti na vicāraṇakkhamaṃ tathā ti idampi so hi caturāsīti satasahassānīti vattumasakkonto evaṃ vadati saddaracakā pana caturāsītiyā tulopo cassa cu rassa lo dvittañcāti vadanti ti etappamāṇavatā mahāsarato sattamahāsaratoti vuttaṃ hoti ti tassa vādānussavane nipāto  kasmā sattānaṃ saṃsaraṇakālassa niyatabhāvato
acelakavatena vā aññena vā yena kenacīti vuttamatidisati ti iminā ti tapakaraṇena etthāpi tādisenevāti adhikāro yo visujjhati so aparipakkaṃ kammaṃ paripāceti nāmāti yojanā ti caturāsītimahākappasatasahassānamabbhantare ti patvā patvā nti caturāsītimahākappasatasahassapamāṇaṃ kālaṃ idaṃ vuttaṃ hoti   saṃsaraṇanimittaṃ kammaṃ sīlādinā sīghaṃyeva visuddhappattiyā  kammaṃ phussa phussa kālena paripakkabhāvānāpādanena  vigamanaṃ ti ti pariminanadoṇatumbena rūpakavasenattho labbhatīti vuttaṃ ti na hāpanavaḍḍhanaṃ paṇḍitabālavasenāti dasseti tiādinā vaḍḍhanaṃ  hāpanaṃ 
ti katasuttavaṭṭiyaṃ ti pareti yathā abhisamparāyoti (mahāni 69 cūḷani 85 paṭi ma 34) ra-kārassa pana la-kāraṃ katvā evaṃ vuttaṃ yathā palibuddhoti (cūḷani 15 mi pa 36) so ca curādigaṇavasena gatiyanti vuttaṃ ti imāya upamāya cesa sattānaṃ saṃsāro anukkamena khīyateva na vaḍḍhati paricchinnarūpattāti imamatthaṃ vibhāvetīti āha tiādi ti khīyanaṭṭhāneyeva

nti deyyadhammasīsena dānacetanāyeva vuttā taṃmukhena ca phalanti dasseti nti iminā dinnañhi mukhyato annādivatthu taṃ kathamesa paṭikkhipissati  esa nayo nti etthāpi sabbasādhāraṇaṃ mahādānaṃ  pāhunabhāvena kattabbasakkāro nti ānisaṃsaphalaṃ nissandaphalañca ti sadisaphalaṃ caturaṅgasamannāgate dāne ṭhānantarādipatti viya hi ānisaṃso  dāne (jā 11039) tāṇalābhamattaṃ viya nissando paṭisandhisaṅkhātaṃ sadisaphalaṃ vipāko  ca kammunā laddhabbo vutto phalābhāvameva sandhāya paṭikkhipanato paccakkhadiṭṭho hi loko kathaṃ tena paṭikkhitto siyā ti iminā kāraṇamāha yattha yattha bhavayoniādīsu ṭhitā ime sattā tattha tattheva ucchijjanti nirudayavināsavasena vinassantīti attho ti mātāpitūsu  na mātāpitūnaṃ nāpi tesu idāni kariyamānasakkārāsakkārānamabhāvavasena tesaṃ loke paccakkhattā pubbuḷassa viya imesaṃ sattānaṃ uppādo nāma kevalo na cavitvā āgamanapubbako atthīti dassanatthaṃ  natthi sattā opapātikāti vuttanti āha ti samaṇena nāma yāthāvato jānantena kassaci akathetvā saññatena bhavitabbaṃ aññathā ahopurisikā nāma siyā kiñhi paro parassa karissati tathā ca attano sampādanassa kassaci avassayo eva na siyā tattha tattheva ucchijjanatoti imamatthaṃ sandhāya ti āha ayaṃ aṭṭhakathāvasesako attho
catūsu mahābhūtesu niyutto  atthamattato pana dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ yathā hi mattikāya nibbattaṃ bhājanaṃ mattikāmayaṃ evamayampi catūhi mahābhūtehi nibbatto catumahābhūtamayoti vuccati ti sattasantānagatā pathavīdhātu nti bahiddhā mahāpathaviṃ tena pathavīyeva kāyoti dasseti ti anubandhati ti padadvayenapi ti bāhirapathavikāyato tadekadesabhūtā pathavī āgantvā ajjhattikabhāvappatti hutvā sattabhāvena saṇṭhitā sā ca mahāpathavī ghaṭādigatapathavī viya idāni tameva bāhiraṃ pathavikāyaṃ samudāyabhūtaṃ puna upeti upagacchati sabbaso tena bāhirapathavikāyena nibbisesataṃ ekībhāvameva gacchatīti attho ti ettha pajjunnena mahāsamuddato gahitaāpo viya vassodakabhāvena punapi mahāsamuddaṃ sūriyaraṃsito gahitaindaggisaṅkhātatejo viya punapi sūriyaraṃsiṃ mahāvāyukkhandhato niggatamahāvāto viya punapi mahāvāyukkhandhaṃ upeti upagacchatīti parikappanāmattena diṭṭhigatikassa adhippāyo
ti manameva chaṭṭhaṃ yesaṃ cakkhusotaghānajivhākāyānaṃ tāni indriyāni  tesaṃ visayabhāvāti vadanti visayīgahaṇena hi visayāpi gahitā eva honti kathaṃ gaṇitā mañcapañcamāti āha ti āḷāhanaṃ susānanti atthato ekaṃ ti guṇadosakoṭṭhāsāni  taṃtaṃkiriyāya pajjitabbato ti pārāvatassa nāma pakkhino vaṇṇāni ti pāṭho pārāvatasakuṇassa pattavaṇṇānīti attho ti  chārikāpariyantā tenāha ti āhutisaddenettha dinnaṃ yiṭṭhaṃ hutanti vuttappakāraṃ dānaṃ sabbampi gahitanti dasseti nti iminā virūpekasesaniddeso vā esa ti adhippāyato attho saddato tassa anadhigamitattā evamīdisesu dabbanti muyhantīti dattū bālapuggalā tehi  kiṃ vuttaṃ hotīti āha tiādi pāḷiyaṃ loko atthīti mati yesaṃ te  atthīti cedaṃ nepātikapadaṃ tesaṃ vādo atthikavādo taṃ 
ti tesu yathāvuttesu tīsu micchāvādīsu  akiriyavādibhāvato  sabbena sabbaṃ āyatiṃ upapattiyā paṭikkhipanato nti ca ānisaṃsanissandasadisaphalavasena tividhampi vipākaṃ  sabbaso hetupaṭisedhaneneva phalassāpi paṭisedhitattā nti ca kammaṃ vipākampi so hi ahetū appaccayā sattā saṃkilissanti visujjhanti cāti vadanto kammassa viya vipākassāpi saṃkilesavisuddhīnaṃ paccayattābhāvajotanato tadubhayaṃ paṭibāhati nāma  asati kammasmiṃ vipākābhāvato  asati vipāke kammassa niratthakatāpattito ti vuttatthanidassanaṃ ti sarūpato visuṃ visuṃ taṃtaṃdiṭṭhidīpakabhāvena pāḷiyaṃ āgatāpi tadubhayapaṭibāhakāvāti attho paccekaṃ tividhadiṭṭhikā eva te ubhayapaṭibāhakattā ti hi hetuvacanaṃ hetugabbhattā tassa visesanassa tiādi paṭiññāvacanaṃ tapphalabhāvena nicchitattā tasmā vipākapaṭibāhakattā  kammapaṭibāhakattā  tadubhayapaṭibāhakattā ti yathālābhaṃ hetuphalatāsambandho veditabbo yo hi vipākapaṭibāhanena natthikadiṭṭhiko ucchedavādī so atthato kammapaṭibāhanena akiriyadiṭṭhiko ubhayapaṭibāhanena ahetukadiṭṭhiko ca hoti sesadvayepi eseva nayo
tiādinā tesamanudiṭṭhikānaṃ niyāmokkantivinicchayo vutto tattha nti  pūraṇādīnaṃ ti taṃ diṭṭhidīpakaṃ ganthaṃ yathā  tathā tehi kataṃ uggahetvā paṭhanti ti tassa atthaṃ vicārenti ntiādi vīmaṃsanākāradassanaṃ karoto ucchijjatīti evaṃ vīmaṃsantānaṃ tesanti sambandho ti yathāparikappite kammaphalābhāvādike karoto na karīyati pāpantiādi nayappavattāya micchādassanasaṅkhātāya laddhiyā ārammaṇe ti micchāsatisaṅkhātā laddhisahagatā taṇhā santiṭṭhati karoto na karīyati pāpantiādivasena hi anussavūpaladdhe atthe tadākāraparivitakkanehi saviggahe viya sarūpato cittassa paccupaṭṭhite cirakālaparicayena evametanti nijjhānakkhamabhāvūpagamane nijjhānakkhantiyā ca tathā tathā gahite punappunaṃ tatheva āsevantassa bahulīkarontassa micchāvitakkena samānīyamānā micchāvāyāmupatthambhitā ataṃsabhāvampi taṃsabhāvanti gaṇhantī micchāladdhisahagatā taṇhā musā vitathaṃ saraṇato pavattanato micchāsatīti vuccati mpi (a ni aṭṭha 2430) cesa attho vuttoyeva micchāsaṅkappādayo viya hi micchāsati nāma pāṭiyekko koci dhammo natthi taṇhāsīsena gahitānaṃ catunnampi akusalakkhandhānametaṃ adhivacananti mpi  (ma ni aṭṭha 183) vuttaṃ
ti yathāsakaṃ vitakkādipaccayalābhena tasmiṃ ārammaṇe avaṭṭhitatāya anekaggataṃ pahāya ekaggaṃ appitaṃ viya hoti cittasīsena cettha micchāsamādhi eva vutto so hi paccayavisesehi laddhabhāvanābalo īdise ṭhāne samādhānapatirūpakakiccakaroyeva hoti vālavijjhanādīsu viyāti daṭṭhabbaṃ ti anekakkhattuṃ tenākārena pubbabhāgiyesu javanavāresu pavattesu sanniṭṭhānabhūte sabbapacchime javanavāre satta javanāni javanti ti idaṃ dhammasabhāvadassanameva na pana tasmiṃ khaṇe tesaṃ tikicchā kenaci sakkā kātunti dassanaṃ tesveva ṭhatvā sattamajavanassa avassamuppajjamānassa nivattituṃ asakkuṇeyyattā evaṃ lahuparivatte ca cittavāre ovādānusāsana vasena tikicchāya asambhavato tenāha ti  ti ariṭṭhabhikkhukaṇṭakasāmaṇerasadisā te viya atekicchā anivattino micchādiṭṭhigatikāyeva jātāti vuttaṃ hoti
ti tesu tīsu micchādassanesu ti yassa ekasmiṃyeva abhiniveso āsevanā ca pavattā so ekameva dassanaṃ okkamati ti yassa dvīsu tīsupi vā abhiniveso āsevanā ca pavattā so dve  tīṇipi okkamati etena pana vacanena yā pubbe iti sabbepete atthato ubhayappaṭibāhakātiādinā ubhayappaṭibāhakatāmukhena dīpitā atthato siddhā sabbadiṭṭhikatā sā pubbabhāgiyā yā pana micchattaniyāmokkantibhūtā sā yathāsakaṃ paccayasamudāgamasiddhito bhinnārammaṇānaṃ viya visesādhigamānaṃ ekajjhaṃ anuppattiyā aññamaññaṃ abbokiṇṇā evāti dasseti tiādinā tissannampi diṭṭhīnaṃ samānasāmatthiyataṃ samānaphalatañca vibhāveti saggāvaraṇādinā hetā samānasāmatthiyā ceva samānaphalā ca tasmā tissopi cetā ekassa uppannāpi abbokiṇṇā eva ekāya vipāke dinne itarā tassā anubalappadāyikāyoti daṭṭhabbaṃ tiādiṃ vatvā tiādinā tadevatthaṃ āvikaroti nti nibbānapathabhūtassa ariyamaggassa nivāraṇaṃ ti paṭikkhepatthe nipāto mokkhasaṅkhātaṃ pana nibbānaṃ gantuṃ kā nāma kathāti attho apica ti pā eva paṭhamatarameva mokkhaṃ gantumabhabbo mokkhagamanatopi dūrataramevāti vuttaṃ hoti evamaññatthāpi yathārahaṃ
ti idaṃ vacanaṃ neyyatthameva na nītatthaṃ tathā hi vuttaṃ  nāma  kiṃ panesa ekasmiṃyeva attabhāve niyato hoti udāhu aññasmimpīti ekasmiṃyeva niyato āsevanavasena pana bhavantarepi taṃ taṃ diṭṭhiṃ rocetiyevāti (ma ni aṭṭha 3103) akusalañhi nāmetaṃ abalaṃ dubbalaṃ na kusalaṃ viya sabalaṃ mahābalaṃ tasmā ekasmiṃyeva attabhāve niyatoti tattha vuttaṃ aññathā sammattaniyāmo viya micchattaniyāmopi accantiko siyā na ca accantiko yadevaṃ vaṭṭakhāṇujotanā kathaṃ yujjeyyāti āha  āsevanavasenātiādi tasmā yathā  sakiṃ nimuggopi nimuggo eva bāloti [a ni 715 (atthato samānaṃ)] vuttaṃ evaṃ vaṭṭakhāṇujotanāpi vuttā yādise hi paccaye paṭicca ayaṃ taṃ taṃ dassanaṃ okkanto puna kadāci tappaṭipakkhe paccaye paṭicca tato sīsukkhipanamassa na hotīti na vattabbaṃ tasmā tattha (ma ni aṭṭha 3102) idha ca aṭṭhakathāyaṃ ti yebhuyyaggahaṇaṃ kataṃ iti āsevanavasena bhavantarepi taṃtaṃdiṭṭhiyā rocanato yebhuyyenassa bhavato vuṭṭhānaṃ natthīti katvā vaṭṭakhāṇuko nāmesa jāto na pana micchattaniyāmassa accantikatāyāti nīharitvā ñātabbatthatāya neyyatthamidaṃ na nītatthanti veditabbaṃ yaṃ sandhāya pi arahā ye ca puthujjanā maggaṃ na paṭilabhissanti te rūpakkhandhañca na parijānanti vedanākkhandhañca na parijānissantītiādi  (yama 1khandhayamaka 210) vuttaṃ ti yathāvuttakāraṇena pathavipālako tadatthaṃ samatthetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ
evaṃ micchādiṭṭhiyā paramasāvajjānusārena sotūnaṃ satimuppādento tiādimāha tattha ti yasmā evaṃ saṃsārakhāṇubhāvassāpi paccayo apaṇṇakajāto tasmā parivajjeyyāti sambandho nti kalyāṇadhammavirahitajanaṃ asādhujanaṃ nti āsumāgatahalāhalaṃ ti diṭṭhadhammikasamparāyikaparamatthānaṃ vasena attano guṇehi vuḍḍhikāmo ti paññācakkhunā vividhatthassa passako dhīroti attho

 akaṭāti ettha ta-kārassa ṭa-kārādesoti āha ti samena visamena vā kenacipi hetunā akatā na vihitāti attho tathā ti etthāpi natthi katavidho karaṇavidhi etesanti  padadvayenāpi loke kenaci hetupaccayena nesaṃ anibbattabhāvaṃ dasseti tenāha tiādi ti kassaci iddhimato cetovasippattassa puggalassa devassa issarādino ca iddhiyāpi na nimmitā ti kassaci  animmāpitā kāmaṃ saddato yuttaṃ atthato ca purimena samānaṃ tathāpi pāḷiyamaṭṭhakathāyañca anāgatameva agahetabbabhāve kāraṇanti dasseti ntiādinā
brahmajālasuttasaṃvaṇṇanāyaṃ (dī ni aṭṭha 130)  idamettha yojanāmattaṃ  vañjhāti hi vañjhapasuvañjhatālādayo viya aphalā kassaci ajanakā tena pathavikāyādīnaṃ rūpādijanakabhāvaṃ paṭikkhipati rūpasaddādayo hi pathavikāyādīhi appaṭibaddhavuttikāti tassa laddhi pabbatassa kūṭamiva ṭhitāti  yathā pabbatakūṭaṃ kenaci anibbattitaṃ kassaci ca anibbattakaṃ evametepi sattakāyāti adhippāyo yamidaṃ bījato aṅkurādi jāyatīti vuccati taṃ vijjamānameva tato nikkhamati na avijjamānaṃ itarathā aññatopi aññassa upaladdhi siyā evametepi sattakāyā tasmā ti ti nibbikārabhāvena suppatiṭṭhitattā ti na vikāramāpajjanti vikārābhāvato hi tesaṃ sattannaṃ kāyānaṃ esikaṭṭhāyiṭṭhitatā aniñjanañca attano pakatiyā avaṭṭhānameva tenāha ti nti sabhāvaṃ  avipariṇāmadhammattā eva  sati hi vikāramāpādetabbabhāve upaghātakatā siyā tathā anuggahetabbabhāve sati anuggāhakatāpīti tadabhāvaṃ dassetuṃ pāḷiyaṃ ntiādi vuttaṃ pathavīyeva kāyekadesattā  yathā samuddo diṭṭhoti  kāyasaddassa samūhavācakattā yathā hatthikāyoti jīvasattamānaṃ kāyānaṃ niccatāya nibbikārabhāvato na hantabbatā na ghātetabbatā ca tasmā neva koci hantā ghātetā vā atthīti dassetuṃ pāḷiyaṃ ntiādi vuttaṃ yadi koci hantā natthi kathaṃ tesaṃ satthappahāroti tattha codanāyāha tiādi tattha ti sattannameva saddo hettha nipātamattaṃ nti paharitaṃ ekatodhārādikaṃ  antareneva pavisati na tesu idaṃ vuttaṃ hoti   ahaṃ imaṃ jīvitā voropemīti tesaṃ tathā  hananaghātanādi pana paramatthato nattheva kāyānaṃ avikopanīyabhāvatoti

 cattāro  yāmā bhāgā catuyāmaṃ catuyāmaṃ eva  bhāgattho hi idha -saddo yathā rattiyā paṭhamo yāmoti (saṃ ni aṭṭha 3368) so panettha bhāgo saṃvaralakkhitoti āha ti saṃyamattho vā saddo yamanaṃ saññamanaṃ yāmoti katvā yatattotiādīsu viya hi anupasaggopi saupasaggo viya saññamatthavācako so pana catūhi ākārehīti āha ti ākāro koṭṭhāsoti hi atthato ekaṃ vārito sabbavāri yassāyaṃ  yathā agyāhitoti tenāha ti vārisaddena cettha vāriparibhogo vutto yathā rattūparatoti paṭikkhitto sabbasītodako tapparibhogo yassāti tathā nti sītodakaṃ ti saṃvaralakkhaṇamattaṃ kathitaṃ ti pāpanijjaralakkhaṇaṃ ti kammakkhayalakkhaṇanti imamatthaṃ dassento tiādimāha ti hi sabbappakārena saṃvaralakkhaṇena pāpavāraṇena samannāgato ti sabbena nijjaralakkhaṇena pāpavāraṇena vidhutapāpo ti aṭṭhannampi kammānaṃ khepanena mokkhappattiyā kammakkhayalakkhaṇena sabbena pāpavāraṇena phuṭṭho taṃ patvā ṭhitoti attho dveyeva gatiyo bhavanti anaññātiādīsu (dī ni 1258 234 3199 200 ma ni 2384 398) viya gamusaddo niṭṭhānatthoti vuttaṃ ti mokkhādhigamena uttamamariyādappattacittoti attho kāyādīsu indriyesu saṃyametabbassa abhāvato  atīte hettha ta-saddo saṃyametabbassa avasesassa abhāvato nti pāpavāraṇaṃ sandhāya vuttaṃ ti atthi jīvo so ca siyā nicco siyā aniccoti (dī ni ṭī 1177) evamādimalīnaladdhitāya ti kammapakativibhāgādivisayāpi sabbā nijjhānakkhantiyo ti micchādiṭṭhiyo eva jātā

ti brahmajāle amarāvikkhepavādavaṇṇanāyaṃ (dī ni aṭṭha 161) vuttanayo eva kasmā vikkhepabyākaraṇabhāvato tatheva ca tattha vikkhepavādassa āgatattā

ti telayantena uppīḷetvā iminā rañño ābhogamāha vadato hi ābhogavasena sabbattha atthanicchayo aṭṭhakathācariyā ca tadābhogaññū paramparābhatatthassāvirodhino ca tasmā sabbattha yathā tathā vacanokāsaladdhabhāvamattena attho na vutto atha kho tesaṃ vattumicchitavasenāti gahetabbaṃ evañca katvā tattha tattha atthuddhārādivasena atthavivecanā katāti
ti idāni mayā pucchiyamāno attho yathā tava citte rucceyya tayā citte ruccethāti attho kammatthe hetaṃ kiriyāpadaṃ mayā vā dāni pucchiyamānamatthaṃ tava sampadānabhūtassa roceyyātipi vaṭṭati gharadāsiyā kucchismiṃ jāto  dhanena kīto  bandhaggāhagahito  sāmameva yena kenaci hetunā dāsabhāvamupagato nti hi sayameva nti dāsabhāvaṃ koci dāsopi samāno alaso kammaṃ akaronto kammakāroti na vuccati so pana na tathābhūtoti visesanametanti āha tiādi ti dūradesato āgataṃ ti attano āsannataraṭṭhānupasaṅkamanato pageva puretarameva ti gāravavasena uṭṭhahitvā tiṭṭhati paccuṭṭhātīti vā attho ti sāmikassa nipajjāya pacchā ti rattiyā vibhāyanavelāya seyyato avuṭṭhite ti atītarattiyā paccūsakālato  nti aparāya bhāviniyā rattiyā padosavelāyaṃ yāva niddokkamanaṃ yā atītarattiyā paccūsavelā bhāviniyā ca padosavelā etthantare sabbakiccaṃ katvā pacchā nipatatīti vuttaṃ  hoti ti kiṃ karaṇīyameva kinti pucchāya kātabbato pucchitvā kātabbaveyyāvaccanti attho paṭissaveneva samīpacāritā vuttāti āha ti paṭikuddhaṃ mukhaṃ oloketuṃ na visahatītipi dasseti nti iminā
ti ādhipaccaparivārādisamannāgato padhānadevo viya tena maññe-saddo idha upamatthoti ñāpeti yathā akkhāhataṃ maññe aṭṭhāsi rañño mahāsudassanassa antepuraṃ upasobhayamānanti (dī ni 2245) nti ettha so vata assaṃ ahanti padacchedo so rājā viya ahampi bhaveyyaṃ kenāti ce yadi puññāni kareyyaṃ tenāti atthoti āha ntiādi saddo upamāyaṃ tenāha ti ti uḷārataraṃ puññaṃ sandhāya vuttaṃ aññadā katapuññato uḷārāya pabbajjāya adhippetattā ntipi pāṭhe so rājā viya ayaṃ ahampi assaṃ kathaṃ yadi puññāni kareyyanti atthasambhavato ti vuttaṃ nti hi uttamapurisayoge ahaṃ-saddo appayuttopi ayaṃ-saddena parāmasanato payutto viya hoti so ahaṃ evarūpo assaṃ vata yadi puññāni kareyyanti paṭhamapāṭhassa atthamicchanti keci evaṃ sati dutiyapāṭhe ayamevatthoti avattabbo siyā tattha ayaṃ-saddena ahaṃ-saddassa parāmasanato soti ca parāmasitabbassa aññassa sambhavato nti dānaṃ ti satabhūtaṃ bhāgampi raññā dinnadānaṃ satadhā katvā tattha ekabhāgampīti vuttaṃ hoti nti yāvajīvaṃ dānatthāya ussāhaṃ karontopi satabhāgamattampi dātuṃ na sakkhissāmi tasmā pabbajissāmīti pabbajjāyaṃ ussāhaṃ katvāti attho ti nipāto parivitakkanattheti vuttaṃ nti
ti kāyena saṃvaritabbassa kāyadvārena pavattanakassa pāpadhammassa saṃvaraṇavasena pidahito ussukkavacanavasena panattho vihareyya-padena sambajjhitabbattāti āha ti hutvāti hi seso nti ca kāyakammabhūtānamakusalānaṃ pavesanabhūtaṃ kāyaviññattisaṅkhātaṃ dvāraṃ ti  vācāya saṃvuto manasā saṃvutoti padadvayepi ti ghāsacchādanapariyesane sallekhavasena paramatāya ukkaṭṭhabhāve vā saṇṭhito ghāsacchādanamattameva paramaṃ pamāṇaṃ koṭi etassa  na tato paraṃ kiñci āmisajātaṃ pariyesati paccāsisati cāti  tassa bhāvo tipi aṭṭhakathāmuttako nayo ghasitabbo asitabboti ghāso āhāro ābhuso chādeti paridahati etenāti  nivāsanaṃ apica ghasanaṃ  ābhuso chādīyate ntipi yujjati ti ghāsacchādanatthāyāpi nti ekavīsatividhampi ananurūpamesanaṃ
nti gaṇasaṅgaṇikato pavivitte ṭhitakāyānaṃ sambandhībhūtānaṃ kāyavivekoti sambandho nti jhānābhiratānaṃ nti tāya eva jhānābhiratiyā paramaṃ uttamaṃ vodānaṃ cittavisuddhiṃ pattānaṃ nti kilesūpadhiabhisaṅkhārūpadhīhi accantavigatānaṃ visaṅkhāraṃ vuccati nibbānaṃ tadadhigamanetā  arahanto tesaṃ ti iminā  (mahāni 7 9) āgatabhāvaṃ dasseti ettha ca paṭhamo viveko itarehi dvīhi vivekehi sahāpi vattabbo itaresu siddhesu tassāpi sijjhanato vinā ca tasmiṃ siddhepi itare samasijjhanato tathā dutiyopi tatiyo pana itarehi saheva vattabbo na vinā itaresu siddhesuyeva tassa sijjhanatoti daṭṭhabbaṃ tiādi tadadhippāyavibhāvanaṃ tattha gaṇe janasamāgame sannipatanaṃ  taṃ  vicarati puggalavasena asahāyattā citte kilesānaṃ sannipatanaṃ  taṃ  kilesavasena asahāyattā maggassa ekacittakkhaṇikattā gotrabhuādīnañca ārammaṇakaraṇamattattā na tesaṃ vasena sātisayā nibbutisukhasamphusanā phalasamāpattinirodhasamāpattivasena pana sātisayāti āha ti phalapariyosāno hi nirodho ti samāpajjanavasena antokatvā ti ettha ussukkavacanametaṃ ārammaṇakaraṇena cittacetasikānaṃ nirodhena ca  nibbutipajjanassa adhippetattā ti jānāpetuṃ ussāhakaraṇatthe
ti abhimukhabhāvena netvā nti tathā pabbajjāya viharantaṃ ti nimantanavasena abhiharaṇaṃ cīvarādīhi payojanaṃ sādhessāmīti vacanasesena yojanā tathā yenattho taṃ vadeyyāthāti nti cīvarādīnaṃ lūkhatāya vikalabhāvaṃ ti tadeva abhihāradvayampi nti sabbagelaññāpaharaṇavasena upakārāvahaṃ bhāvino anatthassa ajananavasena paripālanaṃ rakkhāgutti paccuppannassa pana anatthassa  nisedhavasena paripālanaṃ āvaraṇagutti kimatthiyaṃ dhammikanti visesananti āha tiādi ti upacārasīmāya lābhasīmāya vā
 kevalo yadi-evaṃ-saddo pubbe vuttatthāpekkhakoti vuttaṃ tiādi ti evaṃ labbhamāne sati dutiyaṃ upādāya paṭhamabhāvo tasmā paṭhamanti bhaṇanto aññassāpi atthitaṃ dīpeti tadeva ca kāraṇaṃ katvā rājāpi evamāhāti dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ ti paṭhamasaddena aññassāpi atthitādīpaneneva

ti vilekhati kasiṃ karoti ti ettha -saddo appatthoti vuttaṃ ti idaṃ vuttaṃ hoti  gahassa pati  khuddako gahapati  ekasmiññeva gehamatte jeṭṭhakattāti khuddakabhāvo panassa gehavasenevāti katvā ekagehamatteti vuttaṃ tena hi anekakulajeṭṭhakabhāvaṃ paṭikkhipati gahaṃ gehanti ca atthato samānameva saddo balimhīti vuttaṃ nti ti abhinipphādeti sampādeti ti uparūpari uppādanena mahantaṃ sannicayaṃ karoti
kasmā tadubhayampi vuttanti āha tiādi appampi pahāya pabbajituṃ dukkaranti dassanañca pageva mahantanti viññāpanatthaṃ esā hi kathikānaṃ  pakati yadidaṃ yena kenaci pakārena atthantaraviññāpananti appampi pahāya pabbajituṃ dukkarabhāvo pana majjhimanikāye majjhimapaṇṇāsake  (ma ni 2148 ādayo) dīpetabbo vuttañhi tattha seyyathāpi udāyi puriso daliddo assako anāḷhiyo tassassa ekaṃ agārakaṃ oluggaviluggaṃ kākātidāyiṃ naparamarūpaṃ ekā khaṭopikā oluggaviluggā naparamarūpāti vitthāro yadi appampi bhogaṃ pahāya pabbajituṃ dukkaraṃ kasmā dāsavārepi bhogaggahaṇaṃ na katanti āha tiādi ti attānampi sayamanissaro yathā ca dāsassa bhogāpi abhogāyeva parāyattabhāvato evaṃ ñātayopīti dāsavāre ñātiparivaṭṭaggahaṇampi na katanti daṭṭhabbaṃ parivaṭṭati paramparabhāvena samantato āvaṭṭatīti  ñātiyeva tenāha ti

nti  yathā dāsavāre evamevāti vuttaṃ na tathā idha kassakavāre tadavacanaṃ kasmāti anuyuñjeyya ceti attho ti yathā paṭhamadutiyāni sāmaññaphalāni paññattāni tathāyeva paññapetuṃ sakkā nu khoti vutte ti yathāvuttadāsakassakūpamāsadisāhi upamāhi  anantapaṭibhānatāya vicittanayadesanabhāvato ti evaṃ dīpane  anantanayadesanabhāvato savane vā asantosanena bhiyyo bhiyyo sotukāmatājananato sotukāmatāya pariyantaṃ nāma natthīti attho ti desanāya uttaruttarādhikanānānayavicittabhāve satipīti (dī ni ṭī 1189) ācariyena vuttaṃ satipi evaṃ apariyantabhāvetipi yujjati anumānañāṇena nti taṃ ṭhapetvā tadupari visesameva sāmaññaphalaṃ  kasmāti āha tiādi etena imamatthaṃ dīpeti  anekatthā samānāpi saddā vatticchānupubbikāyeva taṃtadatthadīpakāti
 sādhusaddasseva ka-kārena vaḍḍhetvā vuttattā teneva hi sādhukasaddassatthaṃ vadantena sādhusaddo atthuddhāravasena  udāhaṭo tena ca nanu sādhukasaddasseva atthuddhāro vattabbo na sādhusaddassāti codanā nisedhitā ti abhimukhaṃ yācane abhipatthanāyanti attho ti paṭiggahaṇe ti saṃvijjamānaguṇavasena haṃsane tosane udaggatākaraṇeti attho
ti gāthā ummādantījātake (jā 218101) tatthāyamaṭṭhakathāvinicchayapaveṇī  sucaritadhamme rocetīti  dhammaratoti attho tādiso hi jīvitaṃ jahantopi akattabbaṃ na karoti ti paññavā ñāṇasampanno ti mittānaṃ adussanabhāvo adūsako anupaghātakoti (dī ni ṭī 1189) ācariyena vuttaṃ adrubbhotipi pāṭho da-kārassa dra-kāraṃ katvā
ti sātaccakiriyāyaṃ nti āṇāpane ti sāmaññaphalepi ti sādhukasaddassa suṇohi sādhukaṃ manasi karohīti hi sādhukasaddena savanamanasikārānaṃ sātaccakiriyāpi tadāṇāpanampi jotitaṃ hoti āyācaneneva ca uyyojanasāmaññato āṇatti saṅgahitāti na sā visuṃ atthuddhāre vuttā āṇārahassa hi āṇatti  tadanarahassa āyācananti viseso ti sundaratthepi idāni yathāvuttena sādhukasaddassa atthattayena pakāsitaṃ visesaṃ dassetuṃ tassa vā atthattayassa idha yogyataṃ vibhāvetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ ti suggahitaṃ katvā gaṇhanto nti bhāvanapuṃsakaṃ nti pasatthaṃ nti iminā sambandho nti vā savanānuggahaṇe pariyāyavacanaṃ
ti ettha na ārammaṇapaṭipādanalakkhaṇo manasikāro atha kho vīthipaṭipādanajavanapaṭipādanamanasikārapubbake citte ṭhapanalakkhaṇoti dassento ti āha ti yathāvuttamanasikāradvayapubbakāya cittapaṭipāṭiyā ekārammaṇe ṭhapanavasena anuddhatacitto hutvā ti suṇāhi anaggharatanamiva vā suvaṇṇamañjusāya dullabhadhammaratanaṃ citte paṭisāmehītipi attho  tena vuttaṃ ti evaṃ padadvayassa paccekaṃ yojanāvasena atthaṃ dassetvā idāni paṭiyogīvasena dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ tattha  savane niyojanavasena kiriyantarapaṭisedhanato tena sotaṃ odahāti atthaṃ dasseti  manasikārena daḷhīkammaniyojanena aññacintāpaṭisedhanato  sādhukanti visesetvā vuttattā pi esa nayo
ti ettha -saddena tulanatīraṇādike diṭṭhiyā suppaṭivedhe ca saṅgaṇhāti yathādhippetamatthaṃ byañjeti pakāseti sayametenāti vā  sabhāvanirutti saha byañjanenāti  byañjanasampannoti attho sahappavatti hi sampannatā samavāyatā vijjamānatātiādinā anekavidhā idha pana sampannatāyeva tadaññassa asambhavato tasmā saha byañjanenāti nibbacanaṃ katvāpi byañjanasampannoti (dī ni ṭī 1189) attho ācariyena vuttoti daṭṭhabbaṃ yathā taṃ na kusalā akusalā kusalapaṭipakkhāti (dha sa 1) araṇīyato upagantabbato anudhātabbato  catupārisuddhisīlādi saha atthenāti  vuttanayena atthasampannoti attho sādhukapadaṃ ekameva samānaṃ āvuttinayādivasena ubhayattha yojetabbaṃ kathanti āha tiādi  nāma tanti  nāma tassā manasā vavatthāpitāya tantiyā desanā  nāma tantiyā attho  nāma tantiyā tantiatthassa ca yathābhūtāvabodho yasmā cete dhammadesanātthapaṭivedhā sasādīhi viya mahāsamuddo mandabuddhīhi dukkhogāhā alabbhaneyyapatiṭṭhā ca tasmā gambhīrā tena vuttaṃ ti ettha ca paṭivedhassa dukkarabhāvato  dhammatthānaṃ dukkhogāhatā desanāñāṇassa dukkarabhāvato desanāya uppādetumasakkuṇeyyatāya tabbisayañāṇuppattiyā ca dukkarabhāvato paṭivedhassa dukkhogāhatā veditabbā yamettha vattabbaṃ taṃ  vuttameva
suṇāhi sādhukanti ti vadanto na kevalaṃ atthakkamato eva ayaṃ yojanā atha kho saddakkamatopi ubhayattha sambandhattāti dasseti ti idhāpi aññampi diṭṭheva  dhamme sandiṭṭhikaṃ sāmaññaphalaṃ paṇītatarañcāti idamanuvattatīti āha nti vitthārato bhāsananti atthameva daḷhaṃ karoti ntiādinā hi-saddo cettha luttaniddiṭṭho idaṃ vuttaṃ hoti   nāma uddisanaṃ  nāma niddisanaṃ paribyattakathanaṃ tenāyamattho sambhavatīti yathāvuttamatthaṃ sagāthāvaggasaṃyutte  (saṃ ni 1214) gāthāpadena sādhetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ
ti sāḷikāya nigghoso viya yathā sāḷikāya ālāpo madhuro kaṇṇasukho pemanīyo evanti attho nti cetassa visesanaṃ liṅgabhedassapi visesanassa dissanato yathā guṇo pamāṇanti nti ca saddo vuccati paṭibhāti taṃtadākārena dissatīti katvā ti uccārayi vuccati vā kammagabbhañcetaṃ kiriyāpadaṃ iminā cetaṃ dīpeti  āyasmantaṃ dhammasenāpatiṃ thometukāmena desanābhāsanānaṃ visesaṃ dassentena pabhinnapaṭisambhidena  saṅkhittena vitthārenāti ca visesanaṃ kataṃ tenāyamattho viññāyatīti
ti bhāsissāmīti vutte na kira bhagavā saṅkhepeneva desessati atha kho vitthārenapi bhāsissatīti hi taṃ padaṃ sutvāva  sañjātussāho haṭṭhatuṭṭhoti attho ayamācariyassa adhippāyo apica tena hi mahārāja suṇohi sādhukaṃ manasi karohi bhāsissāmīti vuttaṃ sabbampi uyyojanapaṭiññākaraṇappakāraṃ ussāhajananakāraṇaṃ sabbeneva ussāhasambhavato tasmā ti suṇohi sādhukaṃ manasi karohi bhāsissāmīti vutte sabbeheva tīhipi padehi ussāhajātoti attho daṭṭhabbo ti pati assosi bhagavato vacanasamanantarameva pacchā assosi sakkā pana bhantetiādinā vā pucchitvā puna evaṃ bhanteti assosīti attho taṃ pana patissavanaṃ atthato sampaṭicchanamevāti  āha ti teneva hi iti atthoti avatvā ti vuttaṃ
 athassa  bhagavā etadavocāti vacanasambandhamattaṃ dassetvā etaṃ avocāti padaṃ vibhajitvā atthaṃ dassento tiādimāha ti iminā vuccamānaṃ adhikaraṇaṃ tathāgatassa uppattiṭṭhānabhūtaṃ lokamevādhippetanti dasseti ti iminā desassa upadisanaṃ  tasmiṃ yadi sabbattha desopadese athāyamattho na vattabbo avuttepi labbhamānattāti codanāyāha ntiādi sāmaññabhūtaṃ idhasaddaṃ gaṇhitvā svāyanti vuttaṃ na tu yathāvisesitabbaṃ tathā hi vakkhati katthaci padapūraṇamattamevāti (dī ni aṭṭha 1190)  lokasaddena samānādhikaraṇabhāvato ti ca jātikkhettaṃ tatthāpi ayaṃ cakkavāḷo adhippeto  samaṇoti saddantarasannidhānato ayañhi catukaṅguttarapāḷi tattha ti sotāpanno ti sakadāgāmī vuttañhetaṃ tattheva 
katamo ca bhikkhave paṭhamo samaṇo idha bhikkhave bhikkhu tiṇṇaṃ saṃyojanānaṃ parikkhayā sotāpanno hotīti (a ni 4241) katamo ca bhikkhave dutiyo samaṇo idha bhikkhave bhikkhu tiṇṇaṃ saṃyojanānaṃ parikkhayā rāgadosamohānaṃ tanuttā sakadāgāmī hotīti (a ni 4241) ca ādi

ti imissaṃyeva indasālaguhāyaṃ patiṭṭhamānassa ti devabhāvena devo hutvā vā bhūtassa samānassa ti anādarayoge sāmivacanaṃ puna ti kattutthe idañhi sakkapañhato udāhaṭaṃ
 okāsāpadisanassāpi asambhavena atthantarassa abodhanato pubbe vuttaṃ tathāgatassa uppattiṭṭhānabhūtameva sandhāya nti vuttaṃ purimaṃ uyyojanapaṭiññākaraṇavisaye ālapananti  puna ti ālapati arahanti ādayo saddā vitthāritāti yojanā atthato hi vitthāraṇaṃ saddamukheneva hotīti ubhayattha saddaggahaṇaṃ kataṃ yasmā pana aparehipi aṭṭhahi kāraṇehi bhagavā tathāgatotiādinā (udā aṭṭha 18 itivu aṭṭha 38) tathāgata-saddo  arahanti ādayo ca  (visuddhi ṭī 1130) aparehipi pakārehi vitthāritā ācariyena tasmā tesu vuttanayenapi tesamattho veditabbo tathāgatassa sattanikāyantogadhatāya idha pana sattaloko adhippetoti vatvā tatthāyaṃ yasmiṃ sattanikāye yasmiñca okāse uppajjati taṃ dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ ti ettha yaṃ vattabbaṃ taṃ parato āgamissati
ti tassa nigamassa aparena tato bahīti vuttaṃ hoti ti mahāsālato ti abbhantaraṃ majjhimapadeso ti pañcanimittabaddhā sīmā viya pañcahi yathāvuttanimittehi paricchinne ti paṇṇāsayojanehi ūnatiyojanasate ayañhi majjhimajanapado mudiṅgasaṇṭhāno na samaparivaṭṭo na ca samacaturasso ujukena katthaci asītiyojano hoti katthaci yojanasatiko tathāpi cesa kuṭilaparicchedena miniyamāno pariyanta parikkhepato navayojanasatiko hoti tena vuttaṃ ti ti yebhuyyavasena vuttaṃ sunāparantakassa puṇṇattherassāpi mahāsāvakesu pariyāpannattā sunāparantajanapado hi paccantavisayo tathā hi candanamaṇḍalamāḷapaṭiggahaṇe bhagavā na tattha aruṇaṃ uṭṭhapetīti  (ma ni aṭṭha 4397)  (saṃ ni aṭṭha 3488-89) vuttaṃ ti kulabhogissariyādivasena sīlasārādivasena ca sārabhūtā tibrahmāyupokkharasātiādibrāhmaṇā ceva anāthapiṇḍikādigahapatikā ca
ti majjhimapadese tasmiṃyeva uppajjatīti vacane vā ti evaṃnāmikāya paṭhamaṃ saraṇagamanikāya mātuyā catūsu panetesu vikappesu paṭhamo buddhabhāvāya āsannatarapaṭipattidassanavasena  vutto āsannatarāya hi paṭipattiyā ṭhitopi uppajjatīti vuccati uppādassa ekantikattā pageva paṭipattiyā matthake ṭhito dutiyo buddhabhāvāvahapabbajjato paṭṭhāya āsannamattapaṭipattidassanavasena tatiyo buddhakaradhammapāripūrito paṭṭhāya buddhabhāvāya paṭipattidassanavasena na hi mahāsattānaṃ antimabhavūpapattito paṭṭhāya bodhisambhārasambharaṇaṃ nāma atthi buddhatthāya kālamāgamayamāneneva tattha patiṭṭhanato catuttho buddhabhāvakaradhammasamārambhato paṭṭhāya bodhiyā niyatabhāvadassanena bodhiyā hi niyatabhāvappattito pabhuti buddho uppajjatīti viññūhi vattuṃ sakkā uppādassa ekantikattā yathā pana sandanti nadiyoti sandanakiriyāya avicchedamupādāya vattamānappayogo  evaṃ uppādatthāya paṭipajjanakiriyāya avicchedamupādāya catūsupi vikappesu ti vuttaṃ pavattāparatavattamānavacanañcetaṃ catubbidhañhi vattamānalakkhaṇaṃ saddasatthe pakāsitaṃ

yasmā pana buddhānaṃ sāvakānaṃ viya na paṭipāṭiyā iddhividhañāṇādīni uppajjanti saheva pana arahattamaggena sakalopi sabbaññutaññāṇādiguṇarāsi āgato nāma hoti tasmā tesaṃ nipphattasabbakiccattā arahattaphalakkhaṇe uppanno nāmāti  (a ni aṭṭha 11170) vuttaṃ asati hi nipphattasabbakiccatte na tāvatā uppannoti vattumarahati nti catūsu vikappesu sabbapaṭhamaṃ tathāgato sujātāya uppajjati nāmāti vuttaṃ tathāgatassa uppannatāsaṅkhātaṃ atthibhāvaṃ tadeva  buddhabhāvāya āsannatarapaṭipattiyaṃ ṭhitasseva adhippetattā ayameva hi attho mukhyato uppajjatīti vattabbo tenāha ti
ettha ca uppannoti vutte atītakālavasena koci atthaṃ gaṇheyyāti tannivattanatthaṃ uppanno hotīti vuttaṃ uppannā dhammātiādīsu (dha sa tikamātikā 17) viya hi idha uppannasaddo paccuppannakāliko nanu ca arahattaphalasamaṅgīsaṅkhāto uppannoyeva tathāgato pavedanadesanādīni sādheti atha kasmā  yathāvutto arahattamaggapariyosāno uppajjamānoyeva tathāgato adhippeto na hi so pavedanadesanādīni sādheti madhupāyāsabhojanato yāva arahattamaggo tāva tesaṃ kiccānamasādhanatoti na hevaṃ daṭṭhabbaṃ buddhabhāvāya āsannatarapaṭipattiyaṃ ṭhitassa uppajjamānassa gahaṇeneva arahattaphalasamaṅgīsaṅkhātassa uppannassāpi gahitattā kāraṇaggahaṇeneva hi phalampi gahitaṃ tadavinābhāvittā iti pavedanadesanādisādhakassa arahattaphalasamaṅginopi tathāgatassa gahetabbattā neyyatthamidaṃ uppajjatīti vacanaṃ daṭṭhabbanti tathā hi  (a ni aṭṭha 11170) uppajjamāno uppajjati uppannoti tīhi kālehi atthavibhajane dīpaṅkarapādamūle laddhabyākaraṇato yāva anāgāmiphalā uppajjamāno nāma arahattamaggakkhaṇe pana uppajjati nāma arahattaphalakkhaṇe uppanno nāmāti vuttaṃ ayamettha  mati yasmā pana  ekapuggalo bhikkhave loke uppajjamāno uppajjatīti (a ni 1170) suttapadavaṇṇanāyaṃ  imasmimpi sutte arahattaphalakkhaṇaṃyeva sandhāya uppajjatīti vuttaṃ uppanno hotīti ayañhettha atthoti (a ni aṭṭha 11170) āgataṃ tasmā idhāpi arahattaphalakkhaṇameva sandhāya uppajjatīti vuttanti dasseti sabbapaṭhamaṃ uppannabhāvaṃ sandhāyāti iminā tenāha ti nti ca sabbaveneyyānaṃ paṭhamataraṃ arahattaphalavasena uppannabhāvanti attho ti ca iminā arahattaphalakkhaṇavasena atītakālaṃ dassetīti ayameva ca nayo aṅguttaraṭīkākārena  adhippetoti
ti yo so tathāgato arahantiādinā pakittitaguṇo so bhagavā idāni vattabbaṃ imasaddena nidasseti vuccamānatthassa parāmasanato idaṃ vuttaṃ hoti  nayidaṃ mahājanassa sammukhamattaṃ sandhāya imaṃ lokanti vuttaṃ atha kho sadevakantiādinā vakkhamānaṃ anavasesapariyādānaṃ sandhāyāti ntiādinā yathāvākyaṃ padanibbacanaṃ vuttaṃ yathāpadaṃ pana sadevakotiādinā vattabbaṃ ime ca tagguṇasaṃviññāṇabāhiratthasamāsā ettha hi avayavena viggaho samudāyo samāsattho hoti lokāvayavena  kataviggahena lokasamudāyassa yathārahaṃ labbhamānattā samavāyajotakasahasaddayoge hi ayameva samāso viññāyati ti ca pañcakāmāvacaradevehi arūpāvacaradevehi vā ti rūpāvacarārūpāvacarabrahmunā rūpāvacarabrahmunā eva vā bahukattukādīnamiva nesaṃ siddhi ti yathāsakaṃ kammakilesehi pakārena nibbattakattā
evaṃ vacanatthato atthaṃ dassetvā vacanīyatthato dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ  pārisesañāyena itaresaṃ padantarehi visuṃ gahitattā  paccāsattiñāyena tattha hi māro jāto tannivāsī ca yasmā cesa dāmarikarājaputto viya tattha vasitattā pākaṭo tasmā santesupi aññesu vasavattimahārājādīsu pākaṭatarena teneva visesetvā vuttoti ayañca nayo  (ma ni aṭṭha 2290) pakāsitova māraggahaṇena cettha taṃsambandhino devāpi gahitā okāsalokena saddhiṃ sattalokassa gahaṇato evañhi vasavattisattalokassa anavasesapariyādānaṃ hoti mpi paccāsattiñāyena nti paccatthikā eva paccāmittā teyeva samaṇabrāhmaṇā tesaṃ gahaṇaṃ tathā tena bāhirakasamaṇabrāhmaṇaggahaṇaṃ vuttaṃ nidassanamattañcetaṃ apaccatthikapaccāmittānampi tesaṃ iminā gahaṇato nti  pana sāsanikasamaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ gahaṇaṃ veditabbaṃ kāmaṃ sadevakantiādivisesanānaṃ vaseneva sattavisayopi lokasaddo viññāyati samavāyatthavasena tulyayogavisayattā tesaṃ salomako sapakkhakotiādīsu pana vijjamānatthavasena atulyayogavisayepi ayaṃ samāso labbhatīti byabhicāradassanato abyabhicārenatthañāpakaṃ pajāgahaṇanti āha nti na pana lokasaddena sattalokassa aggahitattā evaṃ vuttaṃ tenāha ti sadevakādivacanena upapattidevānaṃ sassamaṇabrāhmaṇīvacanena visuddhidevānañca gahitattā vuttaṃ nti tattha  rājāno  nti sammutidevehi samaṇabrāhmaṇehi ca avasiṭṭhamanussānaṃ gahaṇaṃ ti etesu padesu ti sadevakasamārakasabrahmakapadehi ti sassamaṇabrāhmaṇīsadevamanussapadehi samāsapadatthesu sattalokassapi vuttanayena gahitattā ti vuttaṃ
tiādinā aparampi vacanīyatthamāha arūpinopi sattā attano āneñjavihārena viharanto dibbantīti devāti idaṃ nibbacanaṃ laddhumarahantīti āha ti tenevāha bhagavā  ākāsānañcāyatanūpagānaṃ devānaṃ sahabyatantiādi (a ni 3197) arūpāvacarabhūto okāsaloko sattaloko ca gahitoti attho evaṃ ti etthāpi chakāmāvacaradevalokassa savisesaṃ māravase pavattanato vuttaṃ ti so hi tassa dāmarikassa viya vasapavattanokāso  pārisesañāyena arūpībrahmalokassa visuṃ gahitattā ti khattiyabrāhmaṇagahapatisamaṇacātumahārājikatāvatiṃsamārabrahmasaṅkhātāsu aṭṭhasu parisāsu khattiyādicatuparisavaseneva tadaññāsaṃ sadevakādiggahaṇena gahitattā kathaṃ panettha catuparisavasena manussaloko gahitoti sassamaṇabrāhmaṇinti iminā samaṇaparisā brāhmaṇaparisā ca gahitā sadevamanussanti iminā khattiyaparisā gahapatiparisā cāti pajanti iminā pana imāyeva catasso parisā vuttā catuparisasaṅkhātaṃ pajanti hi idha attho
aññathā gahetabbamāha ti kathaṃ pana gahitoti sassamaṇabrāhmaṇinti iminā samaṇabrāhmaṇā gahitā sadevamanussanti iminā sammutidevasaṅkhātā khattiyā gahapatisuddasaṅkhātā ca avasesamanussāti ito pana aññesaṃ manussasattānamabhāvato  pajanti iminā eteyeva catūhi pakārehi ṭhitā manussasattā vuttā catukulappabhedaṃ pajanti hi idha attho evaṃ vikappadvayepi pajāgahaṇena catuparisādivasena manussānaññeva gahitattā  idāni avasesasattepi saṅgahetvā dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ etthāpi catuparisavasena gahitena manussalokena saha avasesasabbasattaloko gahito sammutidevehi vā saha avasesasabbasattalokoti yojetabbaṃ nāgagaruḷādivasena ca avasesasabbasattaloko idaṃ vuttaṃ hoti  catuparisasahito avasesasuddanāgasupaṇṇanerayikādisattaloko catukulappabhedamanussasahito vā avasesanāgasupaṇṇanerayikādisattaloko gahitoti
ettāvatā bhāgaso lokaṃ gahetvā yojanaṃ dassetvā idāni tena tena visesena abhāgaso lokaṃ gahetvā yojanaṃ dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ tattha ti ukkaṃsagatiparicchedato tabbijānanenāti vuttaṃ hoti paṭhamanayena hi pañcasu gatīsu devagatipariyāpannāva pañcakāmaguṇasamaṅgitāya dīghāyukatāyāti evamādīhi visesehi seṭṭhā dutiyanayena pana arūpino dūrasamugghāṭitakilesadukkhatāya santapaṇītaāneñjavihārasamaṅgitāya ativiya dīghāyukatāyāti evamādīhi visesehi ativiya ukkaṭṭhā ācariyehi pana dutiyanayameva sandhāya vuttaṃ evaṃ paṭhamapadeneva padhānanayena sabbalokassa sacchikatabhāve siddhepi iminā kāraṇavisesena sesapadāni vuttānīti dasseti ntiādinā ti paṭhamapadato paraṃ āhāti sambandho chakāmāvacarissaro tiyeva vutte sakkādīnampi tassa ādhipaccaṃ siyāti āsaṅkānivattanatthaṃ ti vuttaṃ tena sāhasikakaraṇena vasavattāpanameva tassādhipaccanti dasseti so hi chaṭṭhadevalokepi anissaro tattha vasavattidevarājasseva issarattā tenāha bhagavā vare aṭṭhanipāte  tatra bhikkhave vasavattī devaputto dānamayaṃ puññakiriyavatthuṃ atirekaṃ karitvā paranimmitavasavattī deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhātīti (a ni 836) vitthāro mpi vuttaṃ tatra hi vasavattirājā rajjaṃ kāreti māro pana ekasmiṃ padese attano parisāya issariyaṃ pavattento rajjapaccante dāmarikarājaputto viya vasatīti (ma ni 160) tiādi  dasasahassiyaṃ mahābrahmuno vasena vadati ukkaṭṭhaparicchedatoti hi heṭṭhā vuttameva tiādi ekadesena mahānubhāvatādassanaṃ nti seṭṭhaṃ navalokuttaraṃ ti bahukā visuṃ bhūtā vā nti ukkaṃsagatikānaṃ ti bhāvavasena paresamajjhāsayānurūpaṃ sadevakantiādipadānaṃ anukkamo bhāvavasena  anusandhikkamo vā  atthānañceva padānañca anusandhānapaṭipāṭīti attho ayameva vā pāṭho tathāyeva  (pārā aṭṭha verañjakaṇḍavaṇṇanā 1) diṭṭhattā  (sārattha ṭī 1verañjakaṇḍavaṇṇanā) ca vaṇṇitattā vibhāvanānukkamotipi pāṭho dissati so pana tesu adiṭṭhattā na sundaro
idāni porāṇakānaṃ saṃvaṇṇanānayaṃ dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ tattha aññapadena niravasesasattalokassa gahitattā sabbattha nti anavasesapariyādānaṃ vuttaṃ tenāha ti tedhātukasaṅkhāte tayo bhave upagatasatteti attho ti devamārabrahmasahitatāsaṅkhātehi tīhi ākārehi ti sadevakantiādīsu tīsu padesu ti atthavasena saṅgahetvā teyeva tibhavūpage satte sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiṃ sadevamanussanti padadvaye pakkhipatīti ñāpetuṃ ti vuttaṃ ti sadevakattādinā sassamaṇabrāhmaṇībhāvādinā ca tena tena pakārena tibhavūpage satteti vatvā ti vadantā okāsalokena saddhiṃ sattaloko gahitoti dassenti tedhātukameva pariyādinnanti porāṇā panāhūti yojanā
nti attanā aññatthāpohanena antogadhāvadhāraṇena vā tappaṭisedhanamāha ti aparehi anabhijānāpetabbo hutvāti attho ti ya-kāralopaniddeso yathā paṭisaṅkhā yonisoti (ma ni 123 422 224 375 saṃ ni 4120 a ni 658 mahāni 206) vuttaṃ ti abhisaddena na visesanamattaṃ jotitaṃ atha kho visesanamukhena karaṇampīti dasseti ti iminā ti ettha saddena  upamānaatthāpattisaddantarasannidhānasampayogavippayogasahacaraṇādinā kāraṇalesamattena pavedanaṃ saṅgaṇhāti ekappamāṇattā sabbattha appaṭihatañāṇacāratāya hi sabbadhammapaccakkhā buddhā bhagavanto ti saddato atthavacanaṃ ti adhippāyato evaṃ sabbattha vivecitabbo
nti phalasamāpattisukhaṃ ti -saddaggahaṇaṃ phalasamāpattiyā antarā ṭhitikāpi kadāci bhagavato desanā hotīti katvā kataṃ bhagavā hi dhammaṃ desento yasmiṃ khaṇe parisā sādhukāraṃ vā deti yathāsutaṃ vā dhammaṃ paccavekkhati taṃ khaṇampi pubbābhogena paricchinditvā phalasamāpattiṃ samāpajjati yathāparicchedañca samāpattito vuṭṭhāya pubbe  ṭhitaṭṭhānato paṭṭhāya dhammaṃ desetīti aṭṭhakathāsu (ma ni aṭṭha 2387) vuttovāyamattho ti ugghaṭitaññussa vasena appaṃ vā vipañcitaññussa neyyassa ca vasena bahuṃ vā desento kathaṃ desetīti āha tiādi dhammassa kalyāṇatā niyyānikatāya niyyānikatā ca sabbaso anavajjabhāvenevāti vuttaṃ ti ti pariyattidhammassa desakāyattena hi āṇādividhinā atisajjanaṃ pabodhanaṃ desanāti pariyattidhammo vuccati kiñcāpi avayavavinimutto samudāyo nāma paramatthato koci natthi yesu pana avayavesu samudāyarūpena avekkhitesu gāthādisamaññā taṃ tato bhinnaṃ viya katvā saṃsāmivohāramāropetvā dassento nti āha ti paṭipattidhammassa sāsitabbapuggalagatena hi yathāparādhādinā sāsitabbabhāvena anusāsanaṃ tadaṅgavinayādivasena vinayananti katvā paṭipattidhammo sāsananti vuccati atthi sāsanassa ādimajjhapariyosānanti sambandho ti ettha -saddo sambhāvane tena evaṃ appakatarāyapi ādimajjhapariyosānesu kalyāṇatā pageva bahutarāyāti sambhāveti padañcettha gāthāya catutthaṃso yaṃ pādotipi vuccati eteneva tipādikachapādikāsupi yathāsambhavaṃ vibhāgaṃ dasseti evaṃ suttāvayave kalyāṇattayaṃ dassetvā sakalepi sutte dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ tattha nātibahuvibhāgaṃ yathānusandhinā ekānusandhikaṃ  sandhāya ekānusandhikassāti āha itarasmiṃ pana teneva dhammavibhāgena ādimajjhapariyosānā labbhantīti tiādi vuttaṃ nti  ṭhapitaṃ kāladesadesakaparisādiapadisanalakkhaṇaṃ nidānaganthaṃ ti nigamanaṃ upalakkhaṇameva iti yaṃ taṃ vuttaṃ idametaṃ paṭicca vuttanti nigamanassapi gahetabbato saṅgītikārakehi ṭhapitānipi hi nidānanigamanāni satthu desanāya anuvidhānato tadantogadhānevāti veditabbaṃ ti sabbapacchimo anusandhi
tiādinā sāsanassa idha paṭipattidhammataṃ vibhāveti  pana sāsanadhammoti vuttattā 
sabbapāpassa akaraṇaṃ kusalassa upasampadā
sacittapariyodapanaṃ etaṃ buddhāna sāsananti (dī ni 290 dha pa 183 netti 30 50 116 124)
evaṃ  vuttassa satthusāsanassa pakāsako pariyattidhammo eva sīlādiatthavasena kalyāṇattayavibhāvane vutto idha pana paṭipattiyeva tena vakkhati idha desanāya ādimajjhapariyosānaṃ adhippetanti  sāsanasampattibhūtānaṃ uttarimanussadhammānaṃ mūlabhāvato nti anavajjadhammānaṃ ti vipassanā avinābhāvato panettha samādhiggahaṇaṃ mahāvaggasaṃyutte midaṃ (saṃ ni 5381) kāmaṃ sutte ariyamaggassa antadvayavigamena tesaṃ majjhimapaṭipadābhāvo vutto majjhimabhāvasāmaññato pana sammāpaṭipattiyā ārambhanipphattīnaṃ majjhimabhāvassāpi sādhakabhāve yuttanti āha ti sīlasamādhivipassanāsaṅkhātānaṃ ārambhānaṃ phalanibbānasaṅkhātānañca nipphattīnaṃ vemajjhabhāvato ariyamaggo majjhaṃ nāmāti adhippāyo saupādisesanibbānadhātuvasena  anupādisesanibbānadhātuvasena pana  sāsanapariyosānā hi nibbānadhātu maggassa nipphatti phalavasena nibbānasacchikiriyāya ca hoti tato paraṃ kattabbābhāvatoti vā evaṃ vuttaṃ idāni tesaṃ dvinnampi sāsanassa pariyosānataṃ āgamena sādhetuṃ ntiādimāha etadeva  phalaṃ attho yassāti ti piṅgalakocchabrāhmaṇaṃ bhagavā ālapati idañhi majjhimāgame mūlapaṇṇāsake  (ma ni 1312 ādayo) padaṃ etadeva phalaṃ sāraṃ yassāti  niggahitāgamena tathā nti nibbānantogadhaṃ ti dhammadinnāya theriyā visākhagahapatimālapanaṃ idañhi  (ma ni 1460 ādayo) ntiādisaddantarasannidhānato nti vuttaṃ
evaṃ saddapabandhavasena desanāya kalyāṇattayavibhāgaṃ dassetvā tadatthavasenapi dassento tiādimāha atthatopi hi tassādhippetabhāvaṃ -saddena samattheti tathā samatthanamukhena ca atthavasena kalyāṇattayavibhāgaṃ dassetīti atthato panetaṃ dassento yo tasmiṃ tasmiṃ atthe katavidhi saddapabandho gāthāsuttavasena vavatthito pariyattidhammoyeva idha desanāti vutto tassa cattho visesato sīlādi evāti āha ntiādi visesakathanañhetaṃ sāmaññato pana sīlaggahaṇena sasambhārasīlaṃ gahitaṃ tathā maggaggahaṇena sasambhāramaggoti atthattayavasena anavasesato pariyattiatthaṃ pariyādāya tiṭṭhati itarathā hi kalyāṇattayavibhāgo asabbasādhāraṇo siyā ettha ca sīlamūlakattā sāsanassa sīlena ādikalyāṇatā vuttā sāsanasampattiyā vemajjhabhāvato maggena majjhekalyāṇatā nibbānādhigamato  uttari karaṇīyābhāvato nibbānena pariyosānakalyāṇatā ti sīlādidassanena atthavasena hi idha desanāya ādikalyāṇādibhāvo vutto tiādi yathāvuttānusārena sotūnamanusāsanīdassanaṃ
ti yathāvuttākārena kathanā ti dhammakathikassa saṇṭhānaṃ kathanavasena samavaṭṭhānaṃ
 atthavivaraṇā pasaṃsanā vā  niyyānatthavirahato tassā desanāya ti catusatipaṭṭhānādiniyyānatthadesanato ti sithiladhanitādibhedesu dasasu  byañjanesu ekappakāreneva dvippakāreneva vā byañjanena yuttā bhāsā viya ti vivaṭakaraṇatāya oṭṭhe aphusāpetvā uccāretabbato sabbathā oṭṭhaphusanarahitavimuttabyañjanā bhāsā viya ti sabbasseva vissajjanīyayuttatāya sabbathā vissaggabyañjanā bhāsā viya ti sabbasseva sānusāratāya sabbathā bindusahitabyañjanā pārasikādibhāsā viya evaṃ damiḷakirātasavaramilakkhūnaṃ bhāsā viyāti idaṃ paccekaṃ yojetabbaṃ ti ca pārasikādayo sabbāpesā byañjanekadesavaseneva pavattiyā aparipuṇṇabyañjanāti vuttaṃ ti
ṭhānakaraṇāni sithilāni katvā uccāretabbamakkharaṃ pañcasu vaggesu paṭhamatatiyaṃ  tāni asithilāni katvā uccāretabbamakkharaṃ tesveva dutiyacatutthaṃ  dvimattakālamakkharaṃ  ekamattakālaṃ

saññogaparaṃ dīghañca  asaṃyogaparaṃ rassaṃ  ṭhānakaraṇāni niggahetvā avivaṭena mukhena uccāretabbaṃ  parapadena sambajjhitvā uccāretabbaṃ  tathā asambajjhitabbaṃ  ṭhānakaraṇāni vissaṭṭhāni katvā vivaṭena mukhena uccāretabbaṃ tiādīsu evaṃ sithilādivasena byañjanabuddhisaṅkhātassa akkharuppādakacittassa dasahi pakārehi byañjanānaṃ pabhedoti attho sabbāni hi akkharāni cittasamuṭṭhānāni yathādhippetatthassa  ca byañjanato pakāsanato ti byañjanabuddhiyā vā karaṇabhūtāya byañjanānaṃ dasadhā pabhedotipi yujjati
ti amilecchetvā avināsetvā ahāpetvāti attho tadatthamāha ti yamatthaṃ bhagavā ñāpetuṃ ekagāthaṃ ekavākyampi deseti tamatthaṃ parimaṇḍalapadabyañjanāya eva desanāya desetīti vuttaṃ hoti ti paripuṇṇabyañjanadhammadesanato  saddo idha anavasesavācako na avomissatādivācakoti āha nti nti sabbaso puṇṇaṃ taṃ panatthato ūnādhikanisedhananti vuttaṃ nti tattha yadatthaṃ desito tassa sādhakattā anūnatā veditabbā tabbidhurassa pana asādhakattā anadhikatā upanetabbassa vā vodānatthassa avuttassa abhāvato anūnatā apanetabbassa saṃkilesatthassa vuttassa abhāvato anadhikatā nti sabbabhāgavantaṃ nti sabbaso puṇṇameva tenāha ti  taṇhāya saṃkiliṭṭhattā lokehi taṇhāya āmasitabbato  cīvarādayo paccayā tesu agadhitacittatāya ti hitato pharaṇena hitūpasaṃhārena visesanabhūtena  karaṇabhūtāya ti sakalasaṃkilesato vaṭṭadukkhato ca uddharaṇākārasaṇṭhitena kāruññādhippāyenāti vuttaṃ hoti
ito paṭṭhāya dassāmi evañca dassāmīti samādātabbaṭṭhena dānaṃ  paṇḍitapaññattatāya seṭṭhaṭṭhena brahmaṃ brahmānaṃ vā seṭṭhānaṃ cariyanti dānameva  macchariyalobhādiniggahaṇena samāciṇṇattā dānameva ti deviddhi ti pabhā ānubhāvo vā ti mahatā balena vīriyena ca samannāgamo ti varuṇanāgarājānaṃ vidhurapaṇḍitassa ālapanaṃ
