davathu paritāpotha tilako tilakāḷakoti
tilasaṇṭhānaṃ viya jāyatīti hi kāḷo hutvā jāyatīti  idha pana paṇṇattivītikkamasaṅkhātaṃ thullavajjaṃ kāḷakasadisattā  micchāvītikkamasaṅkhātaṃ aṇumattavajjaṃ tilakasadisattā nti  ayaṃ viseso nti tathā uppāditaṃ pītiṃ vigatabhāvena upaṭṭhānato khayavayavasena sammasanaṃ khīyanaṭṭhena hi va vigato viparīto vā hutvā ayanaṭṭhena tipi vuccati  nāma lokuttarabhūmi ti ariyabhūmiokkamanato devatānaṃ vaṇṇabhaṇanato vā tattha tattha devatānaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā tassa yaso patthaṭoti vuttaṃ hoti evañca katvā heṭṭhā vuttaṃ ayasapattharaṇampi devatānamārocanavasenāti gahetabbaṃ
vivitta-saddo janaviveketi āha nti taṃ pana janasaddanigghosābhāvena veditabbaṃ saddakaṇṭakattā jhānassāti dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ janakaggahaṇeneva hi idha jaññaṃ gahitaṃ tathā hi vuttaṃ  yadeva taṃ appanigghosaṃ tadeva taṃ vijanavātanti (vibha 533) nti ca pakatisaddābhāvamāha nti nagaranigghosādisaddābhāvaṃ īdisesu hi byañjanaṃ sāvasesaṃ viya attho pana niravasesoti aṭṭhakathāsu vuttaṃ  (ma ni aṭṭha 3364) pana  evamāha appasaddassa parittapariyāyaṃ manasi katvā vuttaṃ byañjanaṃ sāvasesaṃ siyāti tenāha na hi tassātiādi saddo panettha abhāvatthotipi sakkā viññātuṃ appābādhatañca sañjānāmītiādīsu (ma ni 1225) viyāti tamatthaṃ  (vibha 528) saṃsandanto tiādimāha ti ca mayā saṃvaṇṇiyamānaṃ nissaddataṃ evāti attho ti gāmādīnaṃ samīpepi edisaṃ vivittaṃ nāma pageva dūreti attho nti asaṅkiṇṇaṃ asambādhaṃ yassa senāsanassa samantā gāvutampi aḍḍhayojanampi pabbatagahanaṃ vanagahanaṃ nadīgahanaṃ hoti na koci avelāya upasaṅkamituṃ  sakkoti idaṃ santikepi anākiṇṇaṃ nāma ti sayati ti nisīdati ti iminā -saddassa -saddassa ca adhikaraṇatthabhāvaṃ dasseti -saddena ca tadubhayapadassa catthasamāsabhāvaṃ tiādinā meva āharati
idāni tassāyevatthaṃ senāsanappabhedadassanavasena vibhāvetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ vibhaṅgapāḷiyaṃ nidassananayena sarūpato dassitasenāsanasseva hi ayaṃ vibhāgo tattha  pākāraparicchinno sakalo  āvāso  dīghapāsādo garuḷasaṇṭhānapāsādotipi vadanti  caturassapāsādo  muṇḍacchadanapāsādo  paṭirājūnaṃ paṭibāhanayoggo catupañcabhūmako patissayaviseso  ekakūṭasaṅgahito anekakoṇavanto patissayaviseso aparo nayo   dīghamukhapāsādo  ekapassachadanakagehaṃ tassa kira ekapasse bhitti uccatarā hoti itarapasse nīcā tena taṃ ekachadanakaṃ hoti  āyatacaturassapāsādo  muṇḍacchadanakaṃ candikaṅgaṇayuttaṃ  kevalā pabbataguhā  dvārabandhaṃ pabbhāraṃ sesaṃ vuttanayameva maṇḍapoti sākhāmaṇḍapoti (dī ni ṭī 1216) evaṃ  aṅguttaraṭīkākārena ca  vuttaṃ
 (vibha aṭṭha 527) pana ti samantā parihārapathaṃ antoyeva ca rattiṭṭhānadivāṭṭhānāni dassetvā katasenāsanaṃ ti supaṇṇavaṅkagehaṃ ti dve kaṇṇikāni gahetvā kato dīghapāsādo ti paṭirājādipaṭibāhanatthaṃ iṭṭhakāhi kato bahalabhittiko catupañcabhūmako patissayaviseso ti bhojanasālāsadiso maṇḍalamāḷo  pana ekakūṭasaṅgahito caturassapāsādoti (pārā aṭṭha 2482-487) vuttaṃ nti pabbataṃ khaṇitvā vā pabbhārassa appahonakaṭṭhāne kuṭṭaṃ uṭṭhāpetvā vā katasenāsanaṃ ti bhūmidari vā yattha rattindivaṃ dīpaṃ laddhuṃ vaṭṭati pabbataguhā vā bhūmiguhā vāti vuttaṃ
taṃ āvasathabhūtaṃ patissayasenāsanaṃ viharitabbaṭṭhena vihāraṭṭhānaṭṭhena ca  masārakādicatubbidho  tathā  uṇṇabhisiādipañcavidhā  sīsappamāṇaṃ  vitthārato vidatthicaturaṅgulatā dīghato mañcavitthārappamāṇatā cettha sīsappamāṇaṃ masārakādīni mañcapīṭhabhāvato bhisiupadhānañca mañcapīṭhasambandhato  mañcapīṭhabhūtañhi senāsanaṃ mañcapīṭhasambandhañca sāmaññaniddesena ekasesena vā mañcapīṭhasenāsananti  vuccati  evameva vadati  pana nti mañcapīṭhañceva mañcapīṭhasambandhasenāsanañcāti (dī ni ṭī 1216) vuttaṃ  nāma sudhāparikammakatāya bhūmiyā vaṇṇānurakkhaṇatthaṃ paṭakhaṇḍādīhi sibbetvā katā  nāma sīhabyagghadīpitaracchacammādīsupi yaṃ kiñci cammaṃ  (pāci aṭṭha 112 vi saṅga aṭṭha 82) hi senāsanaparibhoge paṭikkhittacammaṃ na dissati ti yesaṃ kesañci tiṇānaṃ santhāro eseva nayo pi cimilikādi bhūmiyaṃ santharitabbatāya ti ṭhapetvā vā etāni mañcādīni yattha bhikkhū sannipatanti  nāmāti evaṃ vuttaṃ avasesaṃ rukkhamūlādipaṭikkamitabbaṭṭhānaṃ abhisaṅkharaṇābhāvato kevalaṃ sayanassa nissajjāya ca okāsabhūtattā ti vivittaṃ senāsananti iminā senāsanasaddena vivittasenāsanassa vā ādānena vacanena vā gahitameva sāmaññajotanāya visese avaṭṭhānato visesatthinā ca visesassa payujjitabbato
yadevaṃ kasmā araññantiādi puna vuttanti anuyogena tiādimāha evaṃ gahitesupi senāsanesu yathāvuttassa bhikkhuno anucchavikameva senāsanaṃ dassetukāmattā puna evaṃ vuttanti adhippāyo nti idaṃ vinaye āgatameva sandhāya vuttaṃ na abhidhamme vinaye hi  (pāci 691) bhikkhunīnaṃ āraññakadhutaṅgassa paṭikkhittattā idampi ca tāsaṃ araññaṃ nāma na pana pañcadhanusatikaṃ pacchimaṃ araññameva senāsanaṃ idampi ca tāsaṃ gaṇamhāohīyanāpattikaraṃ na tu pañcadhanusatikādimeva araññaṃ vuttañhi tattha 
ekā vā gaṇamhā ohīyeyyāti agāmake araññe dutiyikāya bhikkhuniyā dassanūpacāraṃ vā savanūpacāraṃ vā vijahantiyā āpatti thullaccayassa vijahite āpatti saṅghādisesassāti
pi (pāci aṭṭha 692) hi tathāva attho vuttoti abhidhamme pana araññanti nikkhamitvā bahi indakhīlā sabbametaṃ araññanti (vibha 529) āgataṃ vinayasuttantā hi ubhopi pariyāyadesanā nāma abhidhammo pana nippariyāyadesanā tasmā yaṃ na gāmapadesantogadhaṃ taṃ araññanti nippariyāyena dassetuṃ tathā vuttaṃ indakhīlā bahi nikkhamitvā  yaṃ ṭhānaṃ pavattaṃ  sabbametaṃ araññaṃ nāmāti cettha attho  suttantanayena  (pārā 652) āraññikaṃ bhikkhuṃ sandhāya vuttaṃ  tasmā  (visuddhi 119) yaṃ  taṃ yuttameva ato tattha vuttanayena gahetabbanti adhippāyo
nti sītacchāyaṃ tenāha tiādi nti rukkhasamīpaṃ vuttañhetaṃ yāvatā majjhanhike kāle samantā chāyā pharati nivāte paṇṇāni nipatanti ettāvatā rukkhamūlanti nti suddhapāsāṇasuddhapaṃsuubhayamissakavasena tividhopi pabbato adhippeto na silāmayo eva -saddo pana avisesato pabbatapariyāyoti katvā evaṃ vuttaṃ tiādinā tadubhayassa anurūpataṃ dasseti ti dasasu disāsu abhimukhībhāvena dissamānāsu tathārūpenapi kāraṇena siyā cittassa ekaggatāti etaṃ vuttaṃ sabbadisāhi āgatena vātena bījiyamānabhāvahetudassanatthanti keci  pipāsavinodanassa kārakattā  taṃ kandaranti apabbatapadesepi vidugganadīnivattanapadesaṃ kandaranti dassetīti (vibha mūlaṭī 530)  teneva viññāyati nadītumbanadīkuñjasaddā nadīnivattanapadesavācakāti nadīnivattanapadeso ca nāma nadiyā nikkhamanaudakena puna nivattitvā gato viduggapadeso apabbatapadesepīti vadanto pana aṭṭhakathāyaṃ nidassanamattena paṭhamaṃ pabbatapadesanti vuttaṃ yathāvutto pana nadīpadesopi kandaro evāti dasseti
tiādināpi nidassanamatteneva tassānurūpabhāvamāha ti puñjaṃ katvā dvinnaṃ pabbatānampi āsannatare ṭhitānaṃ ovarakādisadisaṃ vivaraṃ hoti ekasmiṃyeva pana pabbate umaṅgasadisanti vadanti ācariyā ekasmiṃyeva hi umaṅgasadisaṃ antoleṇaṃ hoti upari paṭicchannattā na dvīsu tathā appaṭicchannattā tasmā umaṅgasadisanti idaṃ ekasmiṃ yevāti iminā sambandhanīyaṃ mahāvivaranti idaṃ pana ubhayehipi nti ca suduṅgāsadisanti (dī ni ṭī 1216)  vuttaṃ ti hi bhūmigharassetaṃ  adhivacanaṃ taṃ gahetvā suduṅgāya ravantaṃ yakkhinī khipītiādīsu viya nti pakatisañcāravasena manussehi na sañcaritabbaṭṭhānaṃ kassanavappanādivasena hi pakatisañcārapaṭikkhepo idhādhippeto tenāha ti saddena pana vanapatthanti vanasaṇṭhānametaṃ senāsanānaṃ adhivacanaṃ vanapatthanti bhīsanakānametaṃ vanapatthanti salomahaṃsānametaṃ vanapatthanti pariyantānametaṃ vanapatthanti na manussūpacārānametaṃ senāsanānaṃ adhivacananti (vibha 531) imaṃ  saṅgaṇhāti ti hi pabbatassa samānabhūmi yo sānūtipi vuccati tassadisattā pana manussānamasañcaraṇabhūtaṃ vanaṃ tasmā patthasadisaṃ vanaṃ ti visesanaparanipāto daṭṭhabbo sabbesaṃ sabbāsu disāsu abhimukho okāso ti āha nti kenaci chadanena antamaso rukkhasākhāyapi na chāditanti attho daṇḍakānaṃ upari cīvaraṃ chādetvā katā ti nīharitvā antopabbhāraleṇasadiso palālarāsiyeva adhippeto itarathā tiṇapaṇṇasanthārasaṅgopi siyāti vuttaṃ ti pabbhārasadise leṇasadise vāti attho ti -saddena purimanayaṃ sampiṇḍeti
piṇḍapātassa pariyesanaṃ  uttarapadalopena tato paṭikkanto ti āha ti nti ettha -saddo samantatoti etasmiṃ atthe tasmā parisamantato aṅkanaṃ āsanaṃ  ra-kārassa la-kāraṃ dvibhāvañca katvā yathā palibuddhoti (mi pa 636) samantabhāvo ca vāmoruṃ dakkhiṇoruñca samaṃ ṭhapetvā ubhinnaṃ pādānaṃ aññamaññasambandhanakaraṇaṃ tenāha nti ūrūnaṃ bandhanavasena nisajjāva idha pallaṅko na āharimehi vāḷehi katoti vuttaṃ hoti ti ca yathā pallaṅkavasena nisajjā hoti tathā ubho pāde ābhugge samiñjite katvā taṃ pana ubhinnaṃ pādānaṃ tathābandhatākaraṇamevāti āha ti nti ettha -saddo uparimakāyavisayo heṭṭhimakāyassa anujukaṃ ṭhapanassa nisajjāvacaneneva viññāpitattāti vuttaṃ ti taṃ pana uparimakāyassa  ujukaṃ ṭhapanaṃ sarūpato dasseti tiādinā aṭṭhārasannaṃ piṭṭhikaṇṭakaṭṭhikānaṃ koṭiyā koṭiṃ paṭipādanameva tathā ṭhapananti adhippāyo
idāni tathā ṭhapanassa payojanaṃ dassento tiādimāha tattha nti tathā ṭhapane sati iminā vā tathāṭhapanahetunā ti na onamanti tiādi pana paramparapayojanadassanaṃ ti evaṃ anonamane ti piṭṭhigilānādivedanā ti na vigacchati vīthiṃ na vilaṅgheti tato eva pubbenāparaṃ visesappattiyā kammaṭṭhānaṃ  parisaddo cettha abhisaddapariyāyo abhimukhatthoti vuttaṃ nti bahiddhā puthuttārammaṇato nivāretvā kammaṭṭhānaṃyeva purakkhatvāti attho parisaddassa samīpatthataṃ dasseti ti iminā mukhassa samīpe viya citte nibaddhaṃ upaṭṭhāpanavasena katvāti vuttaṃ hoti parisaddassa samīpatthataṃ  (vibha 537) sādhetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ ti nāsapuṭagge  nāma uttaroṭṭhassa vemajjhappadeso yattha nāsikavāto paṭihaññati
ettha ca yathā vivittaṃ senāsanaṃ bhajatītiādinā (vibha 508) bhāvanānurūpaṃ senāsanaṃ dassitaṃ evaṃ nisīdatīti iminā alīnānuddhaccapakkhiko santo iriyāpatho dassito pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvāti iminā nisajjāya daḷhabhāvo parimukhaṃ satiṃ upaṭṭhapetvāti iminā ārammaṇapariggahaṇūpāyoti -saddo pariggahaṭṭho pariṇāyikātiādīsu (dha sa 16) viya -saddo niyyānaṭṭho suññatavimokkhamukhantiādīsu viya paṭipakkhato nikkhamanameva hi niyyānaṃ asammosanabhāvo ti paṭisambhidānaye nti sabbathā gahitāsammosatāya pariggahitaṃ pariccattasammosapaṭipakkhatāya ca niyyānaṃ  paramaṃ satinepakkaṃ upaṭṭhapetvāti vuttaṃ hoti ayaṃ  ca mati atha vā kāyādīsu suṭṭhupavattiyā pariggahitaṃ tato eva ca niyyānabhāvayuttaṃ kāyādipariggahaṇañāṇasampayuttatāya vā pariggahitaṃ tatoyeva ca niyyānabhūtaṃ  upaṭṭhānaṃ katvāti atthoti ayaṃ  (vibha mūlaṭī 537) mati
 abhijjhāyati gijjhati abhikaṅkhati etāyāti  kāmacchandanīvaraṇaṃ ti bhijjanaṭṭhena khaṇe khaṇe bhijjanaṭṭhenāti atthoti  (dī ni ṭī 1217)  ca  vuttaṃ suttesu ca dissati luccatīti kho bhikkhu lokoti vuccati kiñca luccati cakkhu kho bhikkhu luccati rūpā luccanti cakkhuviññāṇaṃ luccatītiādi (saṃ ni 482)  (dha sa aṭṭha 7-13) pana idha ca adhunā potthake luccanapaluccanaṭṭhenāti likhitaṃ tattha luccanameva paluccanapariyāyena visesetvā vuttaṃ lucasaddo hi apekkhanādiatthopi bhavati oloketītiādīsu bhijjanapabhijjanaṭṭhenāti attho  pana vuttaṃ khaṇabhaṅgavasena luccanasabhāvato cutibhaṅgavasena ca paluccanasabhāvato loko nāmāti (vaṃsatthapakāsiniyaṃ nāma mahāvaṃsaṭīkāyaṃ paṭhamaparicchede pañcamagāthā vaṇṇanāyaṃ) keci pana bhijjanauppajjanaṭṭhenāti atthaṃ vadanti āhaccabhāsitavacanatthena virujjhanato lucasaddassa ca  anuppādavācakattā ayuttamevetaṃ apica ācariyehipi luccanapaluccanaṭṭhenāti pāṭhameva ulliṅgetvā tathā attho vutto siyā pacchā pana paramparābhatavasena pamādalekhattā tattha tattha na diṭṭhoti daṭṭhabbaṃ na luccati na paluccatīti yo gahitopi tathā na hoti sveva loko aniccānupassanāya vā luccati bhijjati vinassatīti gahetabbova lokoti taṃgahaṇarahitānaṃ lokuttarānaṃ natthi lokatā dukkhasaccaṃ vā lokoti vuttaṃ ti evaṃ tattha tattha vacanatopi yathāvutto kesañci attho na yuttoti
ti pañcupādānakkhandhānameva lokabhāvato ti ettha  tadaṅgappahānavaseneva anuppādanaṃ appavattanaṃ na pana vikkhambhanappahānavasena paṭipakkhānaṃ suṭṭhupahīnaṃ ti hi tathāpahīnasadisataṃ eva sandhāya vuttaṃ kasmāti ce jhānassa anadhigatattā evaṃ pana pubbabhāgabhāvanāya tathā pahānatoyevetaṃ cittaṃ  nāma na  tu cakkhuviññāṇamiva sabhāvato abhijjhāvirahitattāti dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ nti ettha nti nipātamattaṃ  cittaṃ vā adhunā muñcanassa anāgate ca puna anādānassa karaṇaṃ parisodhanaṃ nāmāti vuttaṃ hoti yathā ca imassa cittassa pubbabhāgabhāvanāya parisodhitattā vigatābhijjhatā evaṃ abyāpannatā vigatathinamiddhatā anuddhatatā nibbicikicchatā ca veditabbāti nidassento ti āha ti ābhidosikayavakummāsādayo nti parisuddhapaṇḍarasabhāvaṃ iminā vikāramāpajjatīti atthaṃ dasseti ti purimapakativijahanasaṅkhātena vikāramāpajjanena ntiādinā tulyatthasamāsabhāvamāha yā tasmiṃ samaye cittassa akallatātiādinā (dha sa 1162 vibha 546) thinassa yā tasmiṃ samaye kāyassa akallatātiādinā ca middhassa  niddiṭṭhattā nti vuttaṃ satipi hi thinamiddhassa aññamaññaṃ avippayoge cittakāyalahutādīnaṃ viya cittacetasikānaṃ yathākkamaṃ taṃtaṃvisesassa yā tesaṃ akallatādīnaṃ visesapaccayatā ayametesaṃ sabhāvoti daṭṭhabbaṃ  nāma passito rattiṃ candālokadīpālokaukkālokādi divā ca sūriyālokādi rattimpi divāpi tassa sañjānanasamatthā saññā  tassā ca vigatanīvaraṇāya parisuddhāya atthitā idha adhippetā atisayatthavisiṭṭhassa hi atthiatthassa avabodhako ayamīkāroti dassento tiādimāha vigatathinamiddhabhāvassa kāraṇattā cetaṃ vuttaṃ suttesu pākaṭovāyamattho
saratīti  sampajānātīti ti evaṃ puggalaniddesoti dasseti ti iminā santesupi aññesu vīriyasamādhiādīsu kasmā idameva ubhayaṃ vuttaṃ vigatābhijjhādīsu vā idaṃ ubhayaṃ avatvā kasmā idheva vuttanti anuyogamapanetuṃ ntiādi vuttaṃ puggalādhiṭṭhānena niddiṭṭhasatisampajaññasaṅkhātaṃ idaṃ ubhayanti attho ti ta-saddassa atītatthataṃ āha pubbabhāgabhāvanāya pajahanameva ca atikkamanaṃ kathaṃ idaṃ  kathaṃ idanti pavattatīti  vicikicchā sā etassa atthīti  na kathaṃkathī  nibbicikicchoti vacanattho atthamattaṃ pana dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ kusalesu dhammesūti idaṃ akathaṃkathīti iminā sambajjhitabbanti āha ti ti ettha saddena paccayapahānapahāyakādīnampi saṅgaho daṭṭhabbo tepi hi pabhedato vattabbāti
 vaḍḍhiyā gahitaṃ dhanaṃ iṇaṃ nāmāti vuttaṃ ti vigato anto  so yassāti  tenāha nti virahitadātabbaiṇapariyantaṃ kareyyāti cetassa attho nti vaḍḍhiyā gahitānaṃ iṇadhanānaṃ  taduttari dātabbaiṇaseso natthi iṇamassāti  tassa bhāvo  tameva nidānaṃ  āṇaṇyahetu āṇaṇyakāraṇāti attho āṇaṇyameva hi nidānaṃ kāraṇamassāti vā  pāmojjaṃ somanassanti imehi sambandho iṇapalibodhato muttomhīti  jīvikānimittampi me avasiṭṭhaṃ atthīti 
 nāma dukkhavedanā sā hi kusalavipākasantānassa virodhibhāvato sukhavedanāya visabhāgā tassā  karaṇabhūtāya ti kakacena iva nti catubbidhampi iriyāpathaṃ byādhito hi yathā ṭhānagamanesu asamattho evaṃ nisajjādīsupi ti pīḷeti vātādīnaṃ vikārabhūtā visamāvatthāyeva ti vuccati tenāha ti ābādhasamuṭṭhānena dukkhavedanāsaṅkhātena dukkhena dukkhito dukkhasamannāgatoti attho dukkhavedanāya pana ābādhabhāvena ādimhi bādhatīti ti katvā ābādhasaṅkhātena mūlabyādhinā  aparāparaṃ sañjātadukkhasaṅkhātena anubandhabyādhinā ti attho gahetabbo evañhi sati dukkhavedanāvasena vuttassa dukkhitapadassa ābādhikapadena visesitabbatā pākaṭā hotīti ayamettha  (dī ni ṭī 1219) vuttanayo adhikaṃ mattaṃ pamāṇaṃ  bāḷhaṃ adhimattaṃ gilāno dhātusaṅkhayena parikkhīṇasarīroti ti adhimattabyādhipīḷitatāya ti na ruccetha kammatthapadañcetaṃ bhattañcassāti ettha assāti kattudassanato mattāsaddo anatthakoti vuttaṃ ti appamattakaṃ vā balaṃ nti pāmojjaṃ somanassañca  rogato muttomhīti  atthi me kāyabalanti pāḷiyā attho

tuṇḍikīre pacitvāna tato bhuñjanti bhojananti (dī ni 3281) ādīsu viya
kaṇo tu kuṇḍako bhaveti (abhidhāne bhakaṇḍe catubbaṇṇavagge 454 gāthā) hi vuttaṃ appako pana kaṇo ti vuccati yathā kālavaṇanti tasmā kākaṇova pamāṇamassāti  kākaṇikameva  khuddakakuṇḍakappamāṇamevāti attho daṭṭhabbo evañhi sati rājadāyo nāma kākaṇikamattaṃ na vaṭṭati aḍḍhamāsagghanikaṃ maṃsaṃ detīti (jā aṭṭha 6umaṅgajātakavaṇṇanāya) vuttena  ca aviruddhaṃ hoti ti khayo bhaṅgo tassa bandhanā muttomhīti āvajjayato tadubhayaṃ hoti tena vuttaṃ labhetha pāmojjaṃ adhigaccheyya somanassanti vacanāvasesaṃ sandhāya tiādi vuttaṃ ti ca paṭhamadutiyapadesu vuttanayeneva ti tatiyādīsu tīsu koṭṭhāsesu ekeko hi upamāpakkho padanti vutto
ti āyatto na seribhāvayutto tenāha ti evamitarasmimpi yena gantukāmo tena kāmaṃ gamo na hotīti sapāṭhasesayojanaṃ dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ nti cetaṃ bhāvanapuṃsakavacanaṃ kāmena vā icchāya gamo  niggahītāgamena ti  ettha -saddassa bhāvatthataṃ dasseti ti iminā aparādhīnatāya attano bhujo viya sakicce esitabbo pesitabboti  sayaṃvasīti nibbacanaṃ bhujo nāma attano yathāsukhaṃ viniyogo so isso icchitabbo etthāti  assāmikoti  vuttaṃ atthamattaṃ pana dassento ti āha attāva attano santako na parassāti vuttaṃ hoti anudakatāya kaṃ pānīyaṃ tārenti etthāti  addhānasaddo ca dīghapariyāyoti vuttaṃ nti
ti byāpādādīni ti dassane nti idāni vuccamānā  yena iṇādīnaṃ upamābhāvo kāmacchandādīnañca upameyyabhāvo hoti so nesaṃ upamopameyyasambandho sadisatāti daṭṭhabbaṃ ti parehi iṇasāmikehi nti pharusavacanādikaṃ kiñcipi paṭisedhetuṃ na sakkoti iṇaṃ dātumasakkuṇattā kasmāti vuttaṃ ntiādi iṇassa titikkhākāraṇattāti attho ti yo puggalo yamhi kāmacchandassa vatthubhūte puggale kāmacchandena rajjati ti taṇhābhūtena kāmacchandena taṃ kāmacchandassa vatthubhūtaṃ puggalaṃ mametanti gaṇhāti sahagatasaddo hettha tabbhāvamatto yāyaṃ taṇhā ponobhavikā nandīrāgasahagatātiādīsu (dī ni 2400 ma ni 1133 480 3373 saṃ ni 51081 mahāva 15 paṭi ma 230) viya ti kāmacchandassa vatthubhūtena puggalena kasmāti āha ntiādi kāmacchandassa titikkhākāraṇattāti attho titikkhāsadiso cettha rāgapadhāno akusalacittuppādo titikkhāti vutto na tu  paramaṃ tapo titikkhātiādīsu (dī ni 291 dha pa 184) viya tapabhūto adosapadhāno cittuppādo ti gharassa sāmikabhūtehi sassusasurasāmikehi itthīnaṃ kāmacchando titikkhākāraṇaṃ hoti viyāti sambandho
tiādinā sesānaṃ rogādisadisatā vuttā tattha pittadosakopanavasena  tassa pittakopanato sabbampi  madhusakkarādikaṃ amadhurabhāvena sampajjatīti vuttaṃ ti ti ṭīkāyaṃ (dī ni ṭī 1223) uddhaṭapāṭho upaddavaṃ karothāti nāmadhātuvasena attho idāni pana tumhehi upaddutāti pāṭho dissati ti ito cito ca āhiṇḍati hīnāya vā āvattati madhusakkarādīnaṃ rasaṃ  nānubhavati na jānāti na labhati ca viyāti sambandho nti sāsanassa rasaṃ sāsanameva vā rasaṃ
nakkhattachaṇaṃ  tenāha nti ti bandhanato pamutto ti sotabbadhammassa
sīghaṃ pavattetabbakiccaṃ  sīghattho hi saddo pāṇātipātotiādīsu (ma ni 2193 vibha 968) viya ti vinayakkame akusalena pakataṃ niṭṭhānaṃ vinicchayaṃ jānātīti  na pakataññū tathā so hi kappiyākappiyaṃ yāthāvato na jānāti tenāha tiādi ti sūkaramaṃsādikepi ti acchamaṃsādisaññāya
ti sākhādaṇḍakasaddenapi ti avasaṅkito ceva samantato saṅkito ca ativiya saṅkitoti vuttaṃ hoti tadākāradassanaṃ tiādi so hi thokaṃ gacchatipi gacchanto pana tāya ussaṅkitaparisaṅkitatāya tattha tattha  īdise kantāre gate ko jānāti kiṃ bhavissatīti  tasmā ca  tato eva ca ti pariyāyavacanaṃ kāyikadukkhena khedanaṃ vā  cetasikadukkhena pīḷanaṃ nti khemabhūtaṃ bhūmiṃ antasaddassa tabbhāvattā bhayassa khīyanaṃ vā  sova anto paricchedo yassā tathā sā eva bhūmīti  taṃ nibbhayappadesanti attho ti tattha katamā vicikicchā satthari kaṅkhati vicikicchati dhamme saṅghe sikkhāya pubbante aparante pubbantāparante idappaccayatāpaṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu kaṅkhati vicikicchatīti (vibha 915)  vuttesu aṭṭhasu ṭhānesu ti vinicchinitvā saddahitvā vā nti saddheyyavatthuṃ idamevanti saddahanavasena gaṇhituṃ saddahituṃ na sakkotīti attho ti tasmā vuttanayena asakkuṇanato antarāyaṃ karotīti sambandho atthi nu kho natthi nu khoti araññaṃ paviṭṭhassa ādimhi eva sappanaṃ saṃsayo  tato paraṃ samantato uparūpari vā sappanaṃ  ubhayenapi tattheva saṃsayavasena paribbhamanaṃ dasseti tenāha nti evamidanti samantato anogāhananti attho nti araññasaññāya uppannaṃ chambhitabhāvaṃ hadayamaṃsacalanaṃ utrāsanti vuttaṃ hoti upameyyapakkhepi yathārahamesamattho
ti ettha pana appahīnapakkhe vuttanayānusārena sadisatā veditabbā  yadaggena hi kāmacchandādayo iṇādisadisā tadaggena ca tesaṃ pahānaṃ āṇaṇyādisadisatāti idaṃ pana anuttānapadatthamattaṃ  nti aḍḍhataṃ pubbe paṇṇamāropitāya vaḍḍhiyā saha vattatīti nti iṇadānaggahaṇe sallakkhaṇavasena likhitapaṇṇaṃ puna nti iṇayācanavasena sāsanalikhitapaṇṇaṃ ti dhanasambandhābhāvena avilimpanatāya tathā  pariyāyavacanañhetaṃ dvayaṃ atha vā ti vuttanayena avilimpanabhāvena visesanabhūtena ti attho ti asubhanimittassa uggaho asubhabhāvanānuyogo indriyesu guttadvāratā bhojane mattaññutā kalyāṇamittatā sappāyakathāti ime cha dhamme ti brūhetvā attani vā uppādetvā anuppannaanuppādanauppannappahānādivibhāvanavasena mahāsatipaṭṭhānasutte savisesaṃ pāḷiyā āgatattā ti vuttaṃ ti ca imasmiṃ dīghāgame (dī ni 2372 ādayo) saṅgītamāha na majjhimāgame nikāyantarattā nikāyantarāgatopi hi attho ācariyehi aññattha yebhuyyena vuttoti vadanti esa nayo byāpādādippahānabhāgepi ti ārammaṇabhūte parasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ mamāyanābhāvena  pariggahābhāvena  pageva mānusiyānīti sambhāvane -saddo
ti  attano parassa ca ahitakaro ti mettānimittassa uggaho mettābhāvanānuyogo kammassakatā paṭisaṅkhānabahulatā kalyāṇamittatā sappāyakathāti ime cha dhamme ti mahāsatipaṭṭhāneyeva cārittasīlameva uddissa paññattasikkhāpadaṃ ti vuttaṃ -saddena vārittapaṇṇattisikkhāpadaṃ saṅgaṇhāti
ti pavesāpito bandhanāgāraṃ pavesāpitattā aladdhanakkhattānubhavano puriso hi ti vutto nakkhattadivase eva vā tadananubhavanatthaṃ tathā kato puriso evaṃ vuttotipi vaṭṭati nti tato pacchime aññasmiṃ vā nakkhattadivase nti kammakāraṇākāraṇaṃ kammakāraṇakkhaṇaṃ vā nti diṭṭhadhammikādiatthahāpanamukhena mahato anatthassa kārakaṃ ti atibhojane nimittaggāho iriyāpathasamparivattanatā ālokasaññāmanasikāro abbhokāsavāso kalyāṇamittatā sappāyakathāti ime cha dhamme ti yathāvuttasotabbadhammasaṅkhātassa mahassa sādhūnaṃ ratijananato hi dhammopi chaṇasadisaṭṭhena nakkhattanti vutto
uddhaccakukkucce nti parāyattatāpādanena vuttanayena mahato anatthassa kārakaṃ ti bahussutatā paripucchakatā vinaye pakataññutā vuḍḍhasevitā kalyāṇamittatā sappāyakathāti ime cha dhamme balassa balena vā attanā icchitassa karaṇaṃ  tena nti nīvaraṇato nikkhamanapaṭipadaṃ upacārabhāvanameva na paṭhamaṃ jhānaṃ ayañhi upacārabhāvanādhikāro
ti paccatthikavidhamanasamatthena balena balavā vantu-saddassa abhisayatthavisiṭṭhassa atthiyatthassa bodhanato nti hatthagatadhanasāraṃ ti sajjitadhanvādiāvudho sannaddhapañcāvudhoti attho sūravīrasevakajanavasena nti yathāvuttaṃ purisaṃ balavantatāya sajjāvudhatāya saparivāratāya ca ti sammāpaṭipattiyā vibandhakaraṇato vuttanayena ahitakārikā ti bahussutatā paripucchakatā  vinaye pakataññutā adhimokkhabahulatā kalyāṇamittatā sappāyakathāti ime cha dhamme yathā bāhusaccādīni uddhaccakukkuccassa pahānāya saṃvattanti evaṃ vicikicchāyapīti idhāpi bahussutatādayo tayopi dhammā gahitā kalyāṇamittatā pana sappāyakathā ca pañcannampi pahānāya saṃvattanti tasmā tāsu tassa tassa nīvaraṇassa anucchavikasevanatā daṭṭhabbā ti tiṇaṃ bhayavasena na gaṇeti viya ti duccaritacaraṇūpāyabhūtāya vicikicchāya nittharaṇavasena duccaritasaṅkhātaṃ kantāraṃ nittharitvā vicikicchā hi sammāpaṭipattiyā appaṭipajjananimittatāmukhena micchāpaṭipattimeva paribrūhetīti tassā appahānaṃ duccaritacaraṇūpāyo pahānañca duccaritavidhūnanūpāyoti
ti iminā pāmojjaṃ nāma taruṇapītiṃ dasseti sā hi taruṇatāya kathañcipi tuṭṭhāvatthā tuṭṭhākāramattaṃ ti idaṃ pamuditassāti etassa atthavacanaṃ tassattho okkantikabhāvappattāya pītiyā vasena tuṭṭhassāti  vutto evaṃ sati pāmojjapadena okkantikā pītiyeva gahitā siyā ti etassā cattho attano savipphārikatāya attasamuṭṭhānapaṇītarūpuppattiyā ca sakalasarīraṃ khobhayamānā pharaṇalakkhaṇā pīti jāyatīti vutto evañca sati pītipadena pharaṇā pītiyeva gahitā siyā kāraṇaṃ panettha gavesitabbaṃ idha pana aññattha ca taruṇabalavatāmattasāmaññena padadvayassa atthadīpanato yā kāci taruṇā pīti  balavatī  pañcavidhāya vā pītiyā yathākkamaṃ taruṇabalavatāsambhavato purimā purimā  pacchimā pacchimā tipi vadanti ayamettha tadanucchaviko attho ti pāmojjasaṅkhātāya taruṇapītiyā vasena tuṭṭhassa ta-saddo hi atītattho itarathā hetuphalasambandhābhāvāpattito hetuphalasambandhabhāvassa ca vuttattā ti iminā pīti nāma ettha balavapītīti dasseti sā hi attano savipphārikatāya attasamuṭṭhānapaṇītarūpuppattiyā ca sakalasarīraṃ saṅkhobhayamānā jāyati sakalasarīre pītivegassa pītivipphārassa uppādanañcettha saṅkhobhanaṃ
pītisahitaṃ  uttarapadalopena kiṃ pana taṃ mano pīti mano etassāti samāso pītiyā sampayuttaṃ mano yassātipi vaṭṭati tassa atthamattaṃ pana dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ ti idha sabbopi arūpakalāpo adhippeto na pana kāyalahutādīsu viya vedanādikkhandhattayameva na ca kāyāyatanādīsu viya rūpakāyampīti dasseti ti iminā passaddhidvayavaseneva hettha passambhanamadhippetaṃ passambhanaṃ pana vigatakilesadarathatāti āha ti pahīnauddhaccādikilesadarathoti attho vuttappakārāya pubbabhāgabhāvanāya vasena cetasikasukhaṃ paṭisaṃvedentoyeva taṃsamuṭṭhānapaṇītarūpaphuṭasarīratāya kāyikampi sukhaṃ paṭisaṃvedetīti vuttaṃ ti ti sukhaṃ vedetīti evaṃ vuttena saṃkilesanīvaraṇapakkhato nikkhantattā paṭhamajjhānapakkhikattā ca yathārahaṃ nekkhammasaṅkhātena upacārasukhena appanāsukhena ca samādhānampettha tadubhayenevāti vuttaṃ ti
ettha panāyamadhippāyo  kāmacchandappahānato paṭṭhāya yāva passaddhakāyassa sukhapaṭisaṃvedanā tāva yathā pubbe tathā idhāpi pubbabhāgabhāvanāyeva vuttā na appanā tathā hi kāmacchandappahāne  vuttaṃ vikkhambhanavasenāti ettha vikkhambhanaṃ anuppādanaṃ appavattanaṃ na paṭipakkhānaṃ suppahīnatā pahīnattāti ca pahīnasadisataṃ sandhāya vuttaṃ jhānassa anadhigatattāti (dī ni ṭī 1261) passaddhakāyassa sukhapaṭisaṃvedanāya ca vuttappakārāya pubbabhāgabhāvanāya vasena cetasikasukhaṃ paṭisaṃvedentoyeva taṃsamuṭṭhānapaṇītarūpaphuṭasarīratāya kāyikampi sukhaṃ paṭisaṃvedetīti apica kā nāma kathā aññehi vattabbā aṭṭhakathāyameva cha dhamme bhāvetvāti tattha tattha pubbabhāgabhāvanāya vuttattā sukhino cittasamādhāne pana sukhassa upacārabhāvanāya viya appanāyapi kāraṇattā so vivicceva kāmehītiādinā ca vakkhamānāya appanāya hetuphalavasena sambajjhanato pubbabhāgasamādhi  appanāsamādhi ca vutto pubbabhāgasukhamiva vā appanāsukhampi appanāsamādhissa kāraṇamevāti tampi appanāsukhaṃ appanāsamādhino  kāraṇabhāvena  gahitanti imamatthamasallakkhentā nekkhammapadatthaṃ yathātathaṃ aggahetvā pāḷiyaṃ aṭṭhakathāyampi saṃkiṇṇākulaṃ keci karontīti

 yadevaṃ sukhino cittaṃ samādhiyatīti eteneva upacāravasenapi appanāvasenapi cittassa samādhānaṃ kathitaṃ siyā evaṃ sante so vivicceva kāmehītiādikā desanā kimatthiyāti codanāya nti vuttaṃ tattha samāhiteti padadvayaṃ dassanatthaṃ vuttanti imehi sambandhitvā samāhitattā tathā dassanatthaṃ vuttanti adhippāyo veditabbo nti upacārasamādhito paṭhamajjhānādisamādhito ca upari pattabbassa paṭhamadutiyajjhānādivisesassa dassanatthaṃ upacārasamādhisamadhigameneva hi paṭhamajjhānādiviseso samadhigantuṃ sakkā na pana tena vinā dutiyajjhānādisamadhigamepi pāmojjuppādādikāraṇaparamparā icchitabbā dutiyamaggādisamadhigame paṭipadāñāṇadassanavisuddhi viyāti daṭṭhabbaṃ ti paṭhamajjhānādiappanāsamādhinā ti yo appanālakkhaṇo samādhi sukhino cittaṃ samādhiyatīti sabbasādhāraṇavasena vutto tassa samādhino nti dutiyajjhānādivibhāgassa ceva paṭhamābhiññādivibhāgassa ca pabhedadassanatthaṃ nti catusantatirūpasamudāyabhūtaṃ cātumahābhūtikakāyaṃ so hi gabbhāsaye karīyatīti katvā karasaṅkhātato pupphasambhavato jātattā ti vuccati ti hi mātu soṇitasaṅkhātapupphassa pitu sukkasaṅkhātasambhavassa ca nāmaṃ tato jāto pana aṇḍajajalābujavasena gabbhaseyyakakāyova kāmaṃ opapātikādīnampi hetusampannānaṃ yathāvuttasamādhisamadhigamo sambhavati tathāpi yebhuyyattā pākaṭattā ca sveva kāyo vuttoti karoti putte nibbattetīti  sukkasoṇitaṃ karena jāto tipi vadanti
nanu ca nāmakāyopi vivekajena pītisukhena tathā laddhūpakārova siyā atha kasmā yathāvutto rūpakāyova idha gahitoti saddantarābhisambandhena adhigatattā abhisandetītiādisaddantarābhisambandhato hi rūpakāyo  eva idha bhagavatā vuttoti adhigamīyati tasseva abhisandanādikiriyāyogyattāti ti abhisandanaṃ karoti so  imameva kāyaṃ vivekajena pītisukhenāti hi bhedavasena samudāyāvayavavasena ca parikappanāmattasiddhā hetukiriyā ettha labbhati abhisandanaṃ panetaṃ jhānamayena pītisukhena karajakāyassa tintabhāvāpādanaṃ sabbatthakameva ca lūkhabhāvassāpanayananti āha ti avassutabhāvaṃ allabhāvañca karotīti attho atthato pana abhisandanaṃ nāma yathāvuttapītisukhasamuṭṭhānehi paṇītarūpehi kāyassa parippharaṇaṃ daṭṭhabbaṃ tenevāha ti taṃsamuṭṭhānarūpapharaṇavaseneva hi sabbattha pavattapītisukhatā tiādīsupi eseva nayo  nāma cammapasibbakaṃ ti suddhakiriyāpadaṃ tena vuttaṃ ti so imameva kāyaṃ vivekajena pītisukhena samantato phuṭṭho bhavatīti attho phusanakiriyāyevettha upapannā na byāpanakiriyā bhikkhusseva suddhakattubhāvato sabbaṃ etassa atthīti  yathā guṇavāti tassa  avayavāvayavīsambandhe avayavini sāmivacananti saddalakkhaṇena panetassa kiñcīti avayavena sambajjhanato avayavīvisayoyevesa sabbasaddoti mantvā chavimaṃsādikoṭṭhāsasaṅkhātena avayavena avayavībhāvaṃ dassento āha ti ti etassa nti atthavacanaṃ ti kammajarūpasantatiyā pavattiṭṭhāne aphuṭaṃ nāma na hotīti sambandho nti chavimaṃsalohitādikammajarūpamanugataṃ yattha yattha kammajarūpaṃ tattha tattha cittajarūpassāpi byāpanato tena tassa kāyassa phuṭabhāvaṃ sandhāya ti vuttaṃ
ti kusalo taṃ pana kosallaṃ kaṃsathāle nhāniyacuṇṇāni ākiritvātiādisaddantarasannidhānato pakaraṇato ca nhāniyacuṇṇānaṃ karaṇe payojane piṇḍane ca samatthatāvasena veditabbanti dasseti tiādinā saddo pana mahatiyā kaṃsapātiyātiādīsu  (ma ni 161) suvaṇṇe āgato kaṃso upahato yathātiādīsu (dha pa 134) kittimalohe upakaṃso nāma rājā mahākaṃsassa atrajotiādīsu [jā aṭṭha 410164 (atthato samānaṃ)] paṇṇattimatte idha pana yattha katthaci loheti āha ti nanu upamākaraṇamattamevidaṃ atha kasmā kaṃsathālakassa savisesassa gahaṇaṃ katanti anuyogaṃ pariharati ntiādinā ti parimaddetvā piṇḍaṃ karontasseva bhijjati na pana sandanakkhamaṃ hoti anādaralakkhaṇe cetaṃ sāmivacanaṃ kiriyantarassa pavattanakkhaṇeyeva kiriyantarassa pavattanañhi anādaralakkhaṇaṃ paripphosakaṃ paripphosakanti idaṃ bhāvanapuṃsakanti  dasseti ti iminā phusasaddo cettha parisiñcane yathā taṃ vātavuṭṭhisamaye devo ca thokaṃ thokaṃ phusāyatīti (pāci 362) tasmā tato tato nhāniyacuṇṇato upari udakena byāpanakaraṇavasena parisiñcitvā parisiñcitvāti attho anupasaggopi hi saddo saupasaggo viya pakaraṇādhigatassa atthassa dīpako siñcitvā siñcitvāti pana vacanaṃ paripphosakaṃ paripphosakanti etassa sandeyyāti ettha visesanabhāvaviññāpanatthaṃ evamīdisesu sandeyyāti ettha sanda-saddo piṇḍakaraṇeti vuttaṃ ti ti anupavisanavasena gatā upagatā ti parito gahitā samantato phuṭṭhā
antaro ca bāhiro ca padeso tehi saha pavattatīti  nhāniyapiṇḍi tipi pāṭho ma-kāro padasandhivasena āgamo yathāvuttena pariggahitatākāraṇeneva santarabāhiro nhāniyapiṇḍi phuṭā udakasnehenāti āha ti sabbattha pavattanaṃ  bhāvanapuṃsakañcetaṃ sabbapadese hutvā eva phuṭāti attho santarabāhirā phuṭāti ca iminā nhāniyapiṇḍiyā sabbaso udakena temitabhāvamāha na ca paggharaṇīti pana iminā tintāyapi tāya ghanathaddhabhāvaṃ tenāha ntiādi udakassa phusitaṃ phusitaṃ  na ca paggharaṇī sūdanīti attho binduṃ udakaṃ tipi katthaci pāṭho udakasaṅkhātaṃ bindunti tassattho bindusaddo hi byālambambudharabindūtiādīsu viya dhārāvayave evaṃ pana apaggharaṇato hatthenapi dvīhipi tīhipi aṅgulehi gahetuṃ ovaṭṭikāya vā kātuṃ sakkā yadi hi sā paggharaṇī assa evaṃ sati snehavigamanena sukkhattā thaddhā hutvā tathā gahetuṃ kātuṃ vā na sakkāti vuttaṃ hoti ti parivaṭṭulavasena guḷikāvasena sā piṇḍi kātuṃ sakkāti attho

 tāhi tāhi udakasirāhi ubbhijjati uddhaṃ nikkhamatīti  tādisaṃ udakaṃ yassāti  da-kārassa pana ta-kāre kate  imamatthaṃ dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ nadītīre khatakūpako viya ubbhijjanakaudakoti attho ubbhijjanakampi udakaṃ katthaci heṭṭhā ubbhijjitvā dhārāvasena uṭṭhahitvā bahi gacchati na taṃ koci antoyeva patiṭṭhitaṃ kātuṃ sakkoti dhārāvasena uṭṭhahanato idha pana vālikātaṭe viya udakarahadassa antoyeva ubbhijjitvā tattheva tiṭṭhati na dhārāvasena uṭṭhahitvā bahi gacchatīti  viññāyati akhobhakassa sannisinnasseva udakassa adhippetattāti imamatthaṃ sandhāyāha tiādi ti udakarahadassa heṭṭhā mahāudakasirā lohitānugatā lohitasirā viya udakānugato pathavipadeso udakasirāti vuccati ti dhārāvasena uṭṭhahanakaudako ti udakarahadassa anto samatalapadese eva ti ubbhijjitvā tattheva tiṭṭhanakaudako ti bāhirato udakarahadābhimukhaṃ āgamanamaggo nti ruḷhīpadaṃ eko ekāyātiādi (pārā 443 444 452) viyāti vuttaṃ ti nti ettha saddo byāpane vassānassa addhamāsaṃ addhamāsanti attho evaṃ nti etthāpi nti vassanaṃ ti na upavaccheyya vassasaddato cassa siddhīti dasseti ti iminā
sītā  vāridhārāti itthiliṅgapadassa nti napuṃsakaliṅgena atthavacanaṃ dhārasaddassa dviliṅgikabhāvaviññāpanatthaṃ nti khobhanābhāvena sītalaṃ purāṇapaṇṇatiṇakaṭṭhādisaṃkiṇṇābhāvena vā  parisuddhaṃ setaṃ sītanti hi pariyāyo kasmā panettha ubbhidodakoyeva rahado gahito na itareti anuyogamapaneti tiādinā nti uṭṭhahitvā uṭṭhahitvā dhārākiraṇavasena ubbhijjantaṃ vinassantaṃ vā ti āloḷeti ti vassanaṃ ti udakadhārānipātehi ca tatoyeva uṭṭhitaudakapubbuḷakasaṅkhātehi pheṇapaṭalehi ca evaṃ yathākkamaṃ tiṇṇampi rahadānamagahetabbataṃ vatvā ubbhidodakasseva gahetabbataṃ vadati tiādinā tattha ti sammā samaṃ vā nisinnameva aparikkhobhatāya niccalameva suppasannamevāti adhippāyo ti iddhimatā iddhiyā tathā nimmitaṃ iva ti tasmiṃ upamopameyyavacane nti abhisandetītiādikaṃ

tiādi gacchassapi vanassapi adhivacanaṃ idha pana yāva aggā yāva ca mūlāti vacanayogena appekaccānītiādinā uppalagacchādīnameva gahetabbatāya vanamevādhippetaṃ tasmā ti uppalagacchāni ti uppalavanetiādinā attho veditabbo avayavena hi samudāyassa nibbacanaṃ kataṃ ekañhi uppalagacchādi  uppalādiyeva catupañcamattampi pana uppalādivananti voharīyati  pana jalāsayopi uppaliniādibhāvena vutto ti etasmiṃ padattaye etesu vā tīsu uppalapadumapuṇḍarīkasaṅkhātesu atthesu ti uppalameva vuttaṃ setuppalarattuppalanīluppalesūti attho  uppalasaddassa sāmaññanāmavasena tesu sabbesupi pavattanato nti ettha saddo bahupariyāyo satagghī sataraṃsi sūriyotiādīsu viya anekasaṅkhyābhāvato evañca katvā anekapattassāpi padumabhāve saṅgaho siddho hoti nti ca pupphadalamadhippetaṃ vaṇṇaniyamena nti sāsanavohāro loke pana rattaṃ padumaṃ setaṃ puṇḍarīkanti vadanti vuttañhi puṇḍarīkaṃ sitaṃ rattaṃ kokanadaṃ kokāsakoti rattavaṇṇatāya hi kokanāmakānaṃ sunakhānaṃ nādayato saddāpayato tehi ca asitabbato ti ca padumaṃ vuccati yathāha padmaṃ yathā kokanadaṃ sugandhanti ayaṃ panettha vacanattho udakaṃ pāti udake vā plavatīti  paṅke davati gacchati pakārena vā davati viruhatīti  paṇḍaraṃ vaṇṇamassa mahantatāya vā muḍitabbaṃkhaṇḍetabbanti  ma-kārassa pa-kārādivasena muḍisaddañhi muḍarisaddaṃ vā khaṇḍanatthamicchanti saddavidū saddasatthato cettha padasiddhi yāva aggā yāva ca mūlā udakena abhisandanādibhāvadassanatthaṃ pāḷiyaṃ udakānuggatānīti vacanaṃ tasmā udakato na uggatānicceva attho na tu udake anurūpagatānīti āha ti idha pana uppalādīni viya karajakāyo udakaṃ viya tatiyajjhānasukhaṃ daṭṭhabbaṃ

 yasmā pana catutthajjhānacittameva cetasāti vuttaṃ tañca rāgādiupakkilesamalāpagamato nirupakkilesaṃ nimmalaṃ tasmā upakkilesavigamanameva parisuddhabhāvoti āha nti yasmā ca parisuddhasseva paccayavisesena pavattiviseso pariyodātatā suddhantasuvaṇṇassa nighaṃsanena pabhassaratā viya tasmā pabhassaratāyeva pariyodātatāti āha nti vijju viya pabhāya ito cito ca niccharaṇaṃ  yathā ābhassarāti ti ettha odātenāti guṇavacanaṃ sandhāya nti vuttaṃ nti uṇhassa utuno pharaṇadassanatthaṃ kasmāti āha tiādi ti odātavatthena viya savisesaṃ utupharaṇaṃ na hoti appakamattameva hotīti adhippāyo  tenāha ti ti ca etena odātasaddo ettha parisuddhavacano eva gihī odātavatthavasanotiādīsu viya  na setavacano yena kenaci taṅkhaṇadhotaparisuddheneva utupharaṇasambhavatoti dasseti
nanu ca pāḷiyaṃ nāssa kiñci sabbāvato kāyassa odātena vatthena aphuṭaṃ assāti kāyassa odātavatthapharaṇaṃ vuttaṃ na pana vatthassa utupharaṇaṃ atha kasmā utupharaṇaṃ idha vuttanti anuyogenāha tiādi yasmā vatthaṃ viya karajakāyo utupharaṇaṃ viya catutthajjhānasukhaṃ tasmā evamattho veditabboti vuttaṃ hoti etena ca odātena vatthena sabbāvato kāyassa pharaṇāsambhavato upameyyena ca ayuttattā kāyaggahaṇena tannissitavatthaṃ gahetabbaṃ vatthaggahaṇena ca tappaccayaṃ utupharaṇanti dasseti neyyatthato hi ayaṃ upamā vuttā vicitradesanā hi buddhā bhagavantoti yogino hi karajakāyo vatthaṃ viya daṭṭhabbo utupharaṇasadisena catutthajjhānasukhena pharitabbattā utupharaṇaṃ viya catutthajjhānasukhaṃ vatthassa viya tena karajakāyassa pharaṇato purisassa sarīraṃ viya catutthajjhānaṃ utupharaṇaṭṭhāniyassa sukhassa nissayabhāvato tenāha tiādi idañhi yathāvuttavacanassa guṇadassanaṃ ettha ca pāḷiyaṃ parisuddhena cetasāti cetogahaṇena catutthajjhānasukhaṃ bhagavatā vuttanti ñāpetuṃ catutthajjhānasukhaṃ catutthajjhānasukhenāti ca vuttanti daṭṭhabbaṃ nanu ca catutthajjhānasukhaṃ nāma sātalakkhaṇaṃ natthīti saccaṃ santasabhāvattā panettha upekkhāyeva sukhanti adhippetā tena vuttaṃ  upekkhā pana santattā sukhamicceva bhāsitāti (vibha aṭṭha 232 visuddhi 2644 mahāni aṭṭha 27 paṭi ma aṭṭha 1105)
ti paṭhamajjhānādhigamaparidīpanato paṭṭhāya yāva catutthajjhānādhigamaparidīpanā tāvatā vacanakkamena labhanaṃ  so etassāti  rūpajjhānānaṃ lābhī  yathā lābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātasenāsanagilānapaccayabhesajjaparikkhārānanti (saṃ ni 270 udā 38) labhanasīlo vā  kiṃ labhanasīlo rūpajjhānānītipi yujjati evamitarasmimpi na arūpajjhānalābhīti na veditabboti yojetabbaṃ kasmāti vuttaṃ tiādi aṭṭhannampi samāpattīnaṃ upari abhiññādhigame avinābhāvatoti  vuttaṃ hoti ti kasiṇānulomato kasiṇapaṭilomato kasiṇānulomapaṭilomato jhānānulomato jhānapaṭilomato jhānānulomapaṭilomato jhānukkantikato kasiṇukkantikato jhānakasiṇukkantikato aṅgasaṅkantito ārammaṇasaṅkantito  aṅgārammaṇasaṅkantito aṅgavavatthānato ārammaṇavavatthānatoti (visuddhi 2365)  vuttehi imehi cuddasahākārehi satipi jhānesu āvajjanādipañcavidhavasībhāve ayameva cuddasavidho vasībhāvo abhiññā nibbattane ekantena icchitabboti dassentena nti vuttaṃ iminā ca arūpasamāpattīsu ciṇṇavasībhāvaṃ vinā rūpasamāpattīsu eva ciṇṇavasībhāvena samāpatti na ijjhatīti tāsaṃ abhiññādhigame avinābhāvaṃ dassetīti veditabbaṃ
nanu yathāpāṭhameva vinicchayo vattabboti codanaṃ sodheti tiādinā sāvasesapāṭhabhāvato nīharitvā esa vinicchayo vattabboti vuttaṃ hoti yajjevaṃ arūpajjhānānipi pāḷiyaṃ gahetabbāni atha kasmā tāni aggahetvā sāvasesapāṭho bhagavatā katoti sabbābhiññānaṃ visesato rūpāvacaracatutthajjhānapādakattā satipi hi tāsaṃ tathā avinābhāve visesato panetā rūpāvacaracatutthajjhānapādakā tasmā tāsaṃ tappādakabhāvaviññāpanatthaṃ tattheva ṭhatvā desanā katā na pana arūpāvacarajjhānānaṃ idha ananupayogato tenāha ti

 puna caparaṃ mahārāja (pāḷiyaṃ natthi) bhikkhūti vatvāpi kimatthaṃ dassetuṃ soti padaṃ puna vuttanti codanāyāha ti yathārutavasena neyyatthavasena ca vuttāsu aṭṭhasu samāpattīsu ciṇṇavasitāvisiṭṭhaṃ bhikkhuṃ dassetuṃ evaṃ vuttanti adhippāyo nti soti padatthato sesaṃ evaṃ samāhitetiādīsu vattabbaṃ sādhippāyamatthajātaṃ ñeyyaṃ jānātīti  tadeva paccakkhaṃ katvā passatīti  ñāṇameva dassanaṃ na cakkhādikanti  pañcavidhampi ñāṇaṃ tayidaṃ pana ñāṇadassanapadaṃ  sāsane yesu ñāṇavisesesu niruḷhaṃ taṃ sabbaṃ atthuddhāravasena dassento tiādimāha nti ñāṇadassanassa visuddhipayojanāya ti ariyavihārabhūto sukhavihāro ti na kevalaṃ devatārocanameva atha kho tadā bhagavatopi ñāṇadassanaṃ udapādīti attho sattāhaṃ kālaṅkatassa assāti ti gottavasena vuttaṃ  [vimutti (aṭṭhakathāyaṃ)] nāma arahattaphalasamāpatti yasmā vipassanāñāṇaṃ ñeyyasaṅkhāte tebhūmakasaṅkhāre aniccādito  jānāti bhaṅgānupassanato ca paṭṭhāya paccakkhato te passati tasmā yathāvuttaṭṭhena ñāṇadassanaṃ nāma jātanti dasseti tiādinā
ti vipassanābhimukhaṃ cittaṃ tadaññakaraṇīyato nīharitvā haratīti ayaṃ saddato attho adhippāyato pana taṃ dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ tadabhimukhabhāvoyeva hissa tanninnatādikaraṇaṃ taṃ pana vuttanayena aṭṭhaṅgasamannāgate tasmiṃ citte vipassanākkamena jāte vipassanābhimukhaṃ cittapesanamevāti daṭṭhabbaṃ nti tassaṃ vipassanāyaṃ ninnaṃ itaradvayaṃ tasseva vevacanaṃ tassaṃ  vaṅkaṃ  nīcanti attho brahmajāle  odanakummāsehi upacīyati vaḍḍhāpīyati upacayati vā vaḍḍhatīti atthaṃ sandhāya tiādi vuttaṃ ti ettha aniccadhammotiādinā saddo paccekaṃ yojetabbo tattha ti pabhaṅgutāya addhuvasabhāvo ti sarīre duggandhassa vigamāya ti ucchādetabbatāsabhāvo imassa pūtikāyassa duggandhabhāvato gandhodakādīhi ubbaṭṭanavilimpanajātikoti attho ucchādanena hi pūtikāye sedavātapittasemhādīhi garubhāvaduggandhānamapagamo hoti mahāsambāhanaṃ mallādīnaṃ bāhuvaḍḍhanādiatthaṃva hoti aṅgapaccaṅgābādhavinodanatthaṃ pana khuddakasambāhanameva yuttanti āha ti mandasambāhanenāti attho ti parimadditabbatāsabhāvo
evaṃ  aniyamitakālavasena atthaṃ vatvā idāni niyamitakālavasena atthaṃ vadati tiādinā -saddo cettha atthadassanavaseneva atthantaravikappanassa viññāyamānattā na payutto luttaniddiṭṭho vā ti aciravijātakāle sayāpetvā añchanapīḷanādivasena parimaddanadhammoti sambandho nti bhāvanapuṃsakaniddeso tena yathāpamāṇaṃ mandaṃ vā añchanapīḷanādīni dasseti ñcettha ākaḍḍhanaṃ  sambāhanaṃ saddena samiñjanauggamanādīni saṅgaṇhāti ti ucchādanādinā sukhedhitopi ti aniccatādivasena nassati ca ti evaṃ bhindanto ca kiñci payojanaṃ asādhento vippakiṇṇova hoti evaṃ navahi padehi yathārahaṃ kāye samudayavayadhammānupassitā dassitāti imamatthaṃ vibhāvento tiādimāha tattha ti rūpī cātumahābhūtiko mātāpettikasambhavo odanakummāsūpacayo ucchādanadhammo parimaddanadhammoti imehi chahi padehi yuttaṃ tāva hotu majjhe tīhipi padehi kāyassa samudayakathanaṃ tesaṃ tadatthadīpanato rūpī ucchādanadhammo parimaddanadhammoti pana tīhi  tpadehi kathaṃ tassa tathākathanaṃ yuttaṃ siyā tesaṃ tadatthassa adīpanatoti yuttameva tesampi tadatthassa dīpitattā ti hi idaṃ attano paccayabhūtena utuāhāralakkhaṇena rūpena rūpavāti atthassa dīpakaṃ paccayasaṅgamavisiṭṭhe hi tadassatthiatthe ayamīkāro ucchādanadhammo parimaddanadhammoti ca idaṃ padadvayaṃ tathāvidharūpuppādanena saṇṭhānasampādanatthassa dīpakanti ti bhedanadhammo viddhaṃsanadhammoti dvīhi padehi  kāyapariyāpanne hadayavatthumhi nissitattā vipassanācittassa tadā pavattañhi vipassanācittameva idañca me viññāṇanti āsannapaccakkhavasena vuttaṃ  kāyena vinā appavattanato kāyasaññitānañca rūpadhammānaṃ ārammaṇakaraṇato
 suṭṭhu obhāsatīti  pabhāsampanno maṇi tāya eva pabhāsampattiyā maṇino bhadratāti atthamattaṃ dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ parisuddhākarasamuṭṭhānameva maṇino suvisuddhajātitāti āha ti suvisuddharatanākarato samuṭṭhitoti attho ākaraparivisuddhimūlako eva hi  maṇino kuruvindajātiādijātivisesoti idhādhippetassa pana veḷuriyamaṇino viḷūra (vi va aṭṭha 34 ādayo vākyakkhkhndhesu passitabbaṃ) pabbatassa viḷūra gāmassa ca avidūre parisuddhākaro yebhuyyena hi so tato samuṭṭhito tathā hesa viḷūranāmakassa pabbatassa gāmassa ca avidūre samuṭṭhitattā veḷuriyoti paññāyittha devaloke pavattassapi ca taṃsadisavaṇṇanibhatāya tadeva nāmaṃ jātaṃ yathā taṃ manussaloke laddhanāmavasena devaloke devatānaṃ so pana mayūragīvāvaṇṇo vā hoti vāyasapattavaṇṇo vā siniddhaveṇupattavaṇṇo vāti  (vi va aṭṭha 34) vuttaṃ  (vi vi ṭī 1281) pana allaveḷuvaṇṇoti vadanti tathā hissa vaṃsavaṇṇotipi nāmaṃ jātaṃ mañjārakkhimaṇḍalavaṇṇoti ca vutto tatoyeva so idha padese mañjāramaṇīti pākaṭo hoti cakkavattiparibhogārahapaṇītataramaṇibhāvato pana tasseva pāḷiyaṃ vacanaṃ daṭṭhabbaṃ yathāha puna caparaṃ ānanda rañño mahāsudassanassa maṇiratanaṃ pāturahosi so ahosi maṇi veḷuriyo subho jātimā aṭṭhaṃsotiādi (dī ni 2248) pāsāṇasakkharādidosanīharaṇavaseneva parikammanipphattīti dasseti ti iminā
chaviyā eva saṇhabhāvena acchatā na saṅghātassāti āha ti tato ceva visesena pasannoti dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ paribhogamaṇiratanākārasampatti sabbākārasampannatā  tenāha tiādi pāsāṇādīsu dhotatā  kāḷakādiapaharaṇatthāya ceva suttena āvunatthāya ca vijjhitabbatā saddena tāpasaṇhakaraṇādīnaṃ saṅgaho nti āvunitasuttassa vaṇṇasampattiṃ kasmāti vuttaṃ ntiādi tādisasseva āvutassa pākaṭabhāvatoti vuttaṃ hoti
 paccavekkhitabbato  anupavisitvā ṭhitattā  sammadeva tassa dassanato tassa purisassa maṇino āvibhūtakālo viya tassa bhikkhuno kāyassa āvibhūtakālo tannissayassa pākaṭabhāvato suttassāvibhūtakālo viya tesaṃ dhammānamāvibhūtakālo tannissitassa pākaṭabhāvatoti ayamettha upamāsampādane kāraṇavibhāvanā nti katthaci pāṭho idañca viññāṇanti vacanato pana viññāṇanti pāṭhova sundarataro vipassanāviññāṇanti vā bhavitabbaṃ ti vipassanāñāṇābhimukhaṃ cittaṃ nīharitvā
ti veḷuriyamaṇimhi nti kāyasaññitarūpadhammārammaṇānaṃ phassapañcamakānantiādipadattayassetaṃ visesanaṃ atthavasā liṅgavibhattivacanavipariṇāmoti katvā pacchimapadassāpi visesanabhāvato phassapañcamakaggahaṇena sabbacittacetasikaggahaṇena ca gahitadhammā vipassanācittuppādapariyāpannā evāti daṭṭhabbaṃ evañhi tesaṃ vipassanāviññāṇagatikattā āvutasuttaṃ viya vipassanāviññāṇanti heṭṭhā vuttavacanaṃ avirodhitaṃ hoti kasmā pana vipassanāviññāṇasseva gahaṇanti idañca me viññāṇaṃ ettha sitaṃ ettha paṭibaddhanti iminā tasseva vacanato ayaṃ kho me kāyotiādinā hi vipassanāñāṇena vipassitvā tadeva vipassanāñāṇasampayuttaṃ viññāṇaṃ ettha sitaṃ ettha paṭibaddhanti nissayavisayādivasena manasi karoti tasmā tasseva idha gahaṇaṃ sambhavati nāññassāti daṭṭhabbaṃ tenāha ti dhammasaṅgahādīsu (dha sa 2 ādayo) desitanayena pākaṭabhāvato cettha phassapañcamakānaṃ gahaṇaṃ niravasesapariggahaṇato sabbacittacetasikānaṃ yathārutaṃ desitavasena padhānabhāvato vipassanāviññāṇassāti veditabbaṃ kiṃ panete paccavekkhaṇañāṇassa āvibhavanti udāhu puggalassāti paccavekkhaṇañāṇasseva tassa pana āvibhūtattā puggalassāpi āvibhūtā nāma honti tasmā ti vuttanti
yasmā  panidaṃ vipassanāñāṇaṃ maggañāṇānantaraṃ hoti tasmā lokiyābhiññānaṃ parato chaṭṭhabhiññāya ca purato vattabbaṃ atha kasmā sabbābhiññānaṃ puratova vuttanti codanālesaṃ dassetvā pariharanto ntiādimāha idañca maggañāṇānantaranti hi iminā yathāvuttaṃ codanālesaṃ dasseti tattha nti sikhāppattavipassanābhūtaṃ gotrabhuñāṇaṃ sandhāya vuttaṃ tadeva hi arahattamaggassa sabbesaṃ vā maggaphalānamanantaraṃ hoti padhānato pana tabbacaneneva sabbassapi vipassanāñāṇassa gahaṇaṃ daṭṭhabbaṃ avisesato tassa idha vuttattā maggasaddena ca arahattamaggasseva gahaṇaṃ tassevābhiññāpariyāpannattā abhiññāsambandhena ca codanāsambhavato lokiyābhiññānaṃ purato vuttaṃ vipassanāñāṇaṃ tāsaṃ nānantaratāya anupakāraṃ āsavakkhayañāṇasaṅkhātāya pana lokuttarābhiññāya purato vuttaṃ tassā anantaratāya upakāraṃ tasmā idaṃ lokiyābhiññānaṃ parato chaṭṭhābhiññāya ca purato vattabbaṃ kasmā pana upakāraṭṭhāne tathā avatvā anupakāraṭṭhāneva bhagavatā vuttanti hi codanā sambhavati tiādi parihāradassanaṃ tattha ti yadipi ñāṇānupubbiyā maggañāṇassa anantaratāya upakāraṃ hoti evaṃ satipīti attho
ti chaḷabhiññāvasena vutte desanāvāre ti pañcasu lokiyābhiññāsu kathitāsu ākaṅkheyyasuttādīsu (ma ni 165) viya chaṭṭhābhiññāpi avassaṃ kathetabbā abhiññālakkhaṇabhāvena tappariyāpannato na ca vipassanāñāṇaṃ lokiyābhiññānaṃ chaṭṭhābhiññāya ca antarā pavesetvā kathetabbaṃ anabhiññālakkhaṇabhāvena tadapariyāpannato iti etassa vipassanāñāṇassa tāsamabhiññānaṃ antarā vāro natthi tasmā tattha avasarābhāvato idheva rūpāvacaracatutthajjhānānantaraṃ vipassanāñāṇaṃ kathitanti adhippāyo tiādinā atthantaramāha tattha -saddo samuccayattho tena na kevalaṃ vipassanāñāṇassa idha dassane tadeva kāraṇaṃ atha kho idampīti imamatthaṃ samuccinātīti  (dī ni ṭī 1235) vuttaṃ saddavidū pana īdise ṭhāne ca-saddo vā-saddattho so ca vikappatthoti vadanti tampi yuttameva atthantaradassane payuttattā attanā payujjitabbassa hi vijjamānatthasseva jotakā upasagganipātā yathā magganidassane sākhābhaṅgā yathā ca adissamānā jotane padīpāti evamīdisesu hoti cettha 
atthantaradassanamhi  ca saddo yadi dissati
samuccaye vikappe so gahetabbo vibhāvināti
ti  hetugabbhapadaṃ tathā ti ca ti ettha iddhividhañāṇena bheravaṃ rūpaṃ nimminitvā maṃsacakkhunā passatotipi vattabbaṃ evampi hi abhiññālābhino apariññātavatthukassa bhayaṃ santāso uppajjati uccavālikavāsimahānāgattherassa viyāti ācariyena (dī ni ṭī 1235) vuttaṃ yathā cettha evaṃ ti etthāpi iddhividhañāṇena bheravaṃ saddaṃ nimminitvā maṃsasotena suṇatopīti vattabbameva evampi hi abhiññālābhino apariññātavatthukassa bhayaṃ santāso uppajjati uccavālikavāsimahānāgattherassa viya thero hi koñcanādasahitaṃ sabbasetaṃ hatthināgaṃ māpetvā disvā sutvā ca sañjātabhayasantāsoti  (vibha aṭṭha 2882 ma ni aṭṭha 181 visuddhi 2733) vutto aniccādivasena katasammasanassa dibbāya bhayaṃ santāso na uppajjatīti sambandho  nāma vipassanāñāṇena katasammasanatā tassa tena vā sampādanatthanti attho ti catutthajjhānānantarameva tiādinā yathāpāṭhaṃ yuttataranayaṃ dasseti vipassanāya pavattaṃ pāmojjapītipassaddhiparamparāgatasukhaṃ nti jhānābhiññādīhi asammissaṃ visuṃ bhūtaṃ  tenāha bhagavā  
yato yato sammasati khandhānaṃ udayabbayaṃ
labhatī pītipāmojjaṃ amataṃ taṃ vijānatantiādi (dha pa 374)
idhāpi vuttaṃ idampi kho mahārāja sandiṭṭhikaṃ sāmaññaphalaṃ paṇītatarañcāti tasmā pāḷiyā saṃsandanato imameva nayaṃ yuttataranti vadanti ti abhiññānamādimhiyeva

nti ettha pana saddo aparapaññattivikārapadapūraṇanibbattiādīsu anekesvatthesu āgato idha pana nibbattiattheti dassetuṃ nti vuttaṃ abhiññāmanena nibbattitanti atthoti ācariyenāti (dī ni ṭī 1236 237) vuttaṃ visuddhimagge (visuddhi 2397) pana adhiṭṭhānamanena nimmitattā manomayanti āgataṃ abhiññāmanena adhiṭṭhānamanena cāti ubhayathāpi nibbattattā ubhayampetaṃ yuttameva   nāma hatthapādāditaṃtaṃsamudāyaṃ  nāma kapparajaṇṇuādi tasmiṃ tasmiṃ samudāye avayavaṃ ahīnindriyanti ettha paripuṇṇatāyeva ahīnatā na tu appaṇītatā paripuṇṇabhāvo ca cakkhusotādīnaṃ saṇṭhānavaseneva nimmitarūpe hi pasādo nāma natthīti dassetuṃ nti vuttaṃ imināva tassa jīvitindriyādīnampi abhāvo vuttoti daṭṭhabbaṃ ti ca kamaladalādisadisasaṇṭhānamattavasena na rūpābhighātārahabhūtappasādādiindriyavasena sabbaṅgapaccaṅgiṃ ahīnindriyanti vuttamevatthaṃ samatthento tiādimāha ti kulacārittavasena kaṇṇālaṅkārapiḷandhanatthaṃ avijjhitakaṇṇo nidassanamattametaṃ tenāha ti vaṇṇasaṇṭhānāvayavavisesādisabbākārehīti attho ti iddhimatā
ayamevattho pāḷiyampi vibhāvitoti āha nti katthaci pana  nti pāṭho dissati tattha nti iminā atthantaradassanaṃ nivatteti tiādinā pana tassa upamābhāvaṃ samattheti niyatānapekkhena ca yaṃ-saddena muñjamhā īsikantiādivacanameva paccāmasati ti saṇṭhānatopi vaṇṇatopi avayavavisesatopi sadisabhāvadassanatthaṃyeva kathaṃ sadisabhāvoti vuttaṃ tiādi  nāma tiṇaviseso yena kocchādīni karonti pavāheyyāti vacanato anto ṭhitā eva īsikā adhippetāti dasseti ti iminā ti ca kaḷīro  pana kaṇḍanti (visuddhi ṭī 2399) vuttaṃ ti parivaṭṭulāya asikosiyā ti paṭṭikāya karaḍitabbo bhājetabboti  peḷā karaḍitabbo jigucchitabboti  nimmokaṃ idhāpi  nimmokamevāti āha tiādi  nāma peḷā kasmā ahikañcukasseva nāmaṃ na vilīvakaraṇḍakassāti codanaṃ sodheti tiādinā sveva ahinā sadiso tasmā tasseva nāmanti vuttaṃ hoti  pana ti peḷāya nimmokatoti ca vadantīti (visuddhi ṭī 2399) vuttaṃ tattha peḷāgahaṇaṃ ahinā asadisatāya vicāretabbaṃ
yajjevaṃ seyyathāpi pana mahārāja puriso ahiṃ karaṇḍā uddhareyyāti purisassa karaṇḍato ahiuddharaṇūpamāya ayamattho virujjheyya na hi so hatthena tato uddharituṃ sakkāti  anuyogenāha tiādi uddhareyyāti hi aniyamavacanepi hatthena uddharaṇasseva pākaṭattā taṃdassanamiva jātaṃ tenāha ti tiādi cittena uddharaṇassa hetudassanaṃ ahino nāma pañcasu ṭhānesu sajātiṃ nātivattanti upapattiyaṃ cutiyaṃ vissaṭṭhaniddokkamane samānajātiyā methunapaṭisevane jiṇṇatacāpanayaneti vuttaṃ ti uragajātiyameva ṭhito pajahati na nāgiddhiyā aññajātirūpoti attho idañhi mahiddhike nāge sandhāya vuttaṃ ti attanoyeva tacaṃ attano sarīraṃ khādayamānaṃ viya ti jiṇṇatāya katthaci muttaṃ katthaci olambitaṃ jiṇṇatacaṃ jigucchanto ti sajātiyaṃ ṭhito nissāya thāmena jigucchantoti yathāvuttehi catūhi kāraṇehi ti kañcukato ti attato aññena ti purisassa citteneva na hatthena seyyathāpi nāma puriso ahiṃ passitvā aho vatāhaṃ imaṃ ahiṃ kañcukato uddhareyyanti ahiṃ karaṇḍā cittena uddhareyya tassa evamassa ayaṃ ahi ayaṃ karaṇḍo añño ahi añño karaṇḍo karaṇḍā tveva ahi ubbhatoti evameva so imamhā kāyā aññaṃ kāyaṃ abhinimmināti ahīnindriyanti ayamettha adhippāyo

 bhājanādivikatikiriyānissayabhūtā  vikubbanakiriyānissayabhāvato 
 pubbe nīvaraṇappahānavāre viya kantāraggahaṇaṃ akatvā kevalaṃ addhānamaggaggahaṇaṃ khemamaggadassanatthaṃ kasmā pana khemamaggasseva dassanaṃ na kantāramaggassa nanu upamādassanamattametanti codanaṃ pariharanto tiādimāha tiādi pana khemamaggasseva gahaṇakāraṇadassanaṃ vātātapādinivāraṇatthaṃ  tathā tathā pana paripuṇṇavacanaṃ upamāsampattiyā upameyyasampādanatthaṃ adhippetassa ca upameyyatthassa suviññāpanatthaṃ hetudāharaṇabhedyabhedakādisampannavacanena ca viññūjātikānaṃ cittārādhanatthanti veditabbaṃ evaṃ sabbattha ti akicchaṃ akasirena sallakkheti paricchindati ca
 mando uttānaseyyakadārakopi daharoti vuccatīti tato visesanatthaṃ yuvāti  vuttanti mantvā yuvasaddena visesitabbameva daharasaddassa atthaṃ dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ tathā yuvāpi koci anicchanako anicchanato ca amaṇḍanajātikoti tato visesanatthaṃ maṇḍanajātikotiādi vuttanti mantvā maṇḍanajātikādisaddena visesitabbameva yuvasaddassa atthaṃ dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ pāḷiyañhi yathākkamaṃ padattayassa visesitabbavisesakabhāvena vacanato tathā saṃvaṇṇanā katā itarathā ekakenāpi padena adhippetatthādhigamikā saparivārā saṃvaṇṇanāva kātabbā siyāti maṇḍanapakatikoti vuttameva vivarituṃ tiādimāha saddo dosapariyāyo doso ca nāma kāḷatilakādīti dasseti tiādinā kāḷatilappamāṇā bindavo  vā kammāsā ye sāsapabījikātipi vuccanti tilappamāṇā bindavo  nāma viyaṅgaṃ vipariṇāmitamaṅgaṃ yobbannapīḷakādayo  ye kharapīḷakā tipi vuccanti nti mukhacchāyaṃ mukhe gato doso  lakkhaṇavacanamattametaṃ mukhe adosassapi pākaṭabhāvassa adhippetattā yathā vā mukhe doso evaṃ mukhe adosopi ti saralopena vutto sāmaññaniddesatopi anekatthassa viññātabbattā pisaddalopena vā ayamattho veditabbo avuttopi hi attho sampiṇḍanavasena vutto viya viññāyati mukhadoso ca mukhaadoso ca ti ekadesasarūpekasesanayenapettha attho daṭṭhabbo evañhi atthassa paripuṇṇatāya paresaṃ soḷasavidhaṃ cittaṃ pākaṭaṃ hotīti vacanaṃ samatthitaṃ hoti tenetaṃ vuccati 
vattabbassāvasiṭṭhassa gāho nidassanādinā
apisaddādilopena ekasesanayena vā
asamāne sadde tidhā catudhā ca samānake
sāmaññaniddesatopi veditabbo vibhāvināti
sarāgaṃ vā cittantiādinā pāḷiyaṃ vuttaṃ 
nti pubbenivāsañāṇassa pubbenivāsañāṇe vā dassitāya upamāya kasmā pana pāḷiyaṃ gāmattayameva upamāne gahitanti codanaṃ sodhetuṃ ntiādi vuttaṃ taṃ divasaṃ katakiriyā nāma pākatikasattassāpi yebhuyyena pākaṭā hoti tasmā taṃ divasaṃ gantuṃ sakkuṇeyyaṃ gāmattayameva bhagavatā gahitaṃ na taduttarīti adhippāyo  kiñcāpi pāḷiyaṃ taṃdivasaggahaṇaṃ natthi gāmattayaggahaṇena pana tadaheva katakiriyā adhippetāti mantvā aṭṭhakathāyaṃ taṃdivasaggahaṇaṃ katanti daṭṭhabbaṃ taṃdivasagatagāmattayaggahaṇeneva ca mahābhinīhārehi aññesampi pubbenivāsañāṇalābhīnaṃ tīsupi bhavesu katakiriyā yebhuyyena pākaṭā hotīti dīpitanti daṭṭhabbaṃ etadatthampi hi gāmattayaggahaṇanti ti abhisamparāyesu pubbe diṭṭhadhamme pana idāni pubbe ca katakiccassa
 pāḷiyaṃ ti aññāya rathikāya aññaṃ rathiṃ sañcaranteti attho tena aparāparaṃ sañcaraṇaṃ dassitanti āha ti taṃtaṃkiccavasena ito cito ca sañcaranteti vuttaṃ hoti ayamevattho rathivīthisaddānamekatthattā ti vīthicatukke  tattha patiṭṭhitassa daṭṭhabbadassanasiddhito maṃsacakkhumato hi dibbacakkhusamadhigamo yathāha maṃsacakkhussa uppādo maggo dibbassa cakkhunoti (itivu 61)  daṭṭhabbassa dassanato gehaṃ pavisanto tato nikkhamanto viya ca mātukucchiṃ paṭisandhivasena pavisanto tato ca vijātivasena nikkhamanto mātukucchiyā gehasadisattā tathā hi vuttaṃ mātaraṃ kuṭikaṃ brūsi bhariyaṃ brūsi kulāvakanti (saṃ ni 119) ayaṃ aṭṭhakathāmuttako nayo  gehaṃ pavisanto viya attabhāvaṃ upapajjanavasena okkamanto gehā nikkhamanto viya ca attabhāvato cavanavasena apakkamanto attabhāvassa gehasadisattā vuttañhi gahakāraka diṭṭhosi puna gehaṃ na kāhasīti (dha pa 154)
ti punappunaṃ saṃsāre paribbhamanakasattā ti ajjhokāsadesabhūte ti nagarassa majjhabhūte ti tasmiṃ tasmiṃ bhavekadese ti uppajjamānakasattā iminā hi tasmiṃ tasmiṃ bhave jātasaṃvaddhe satte vadati aparāparaṃ sañcaraṇakasattāti pana etena tathā aniyamitakālike sādhāraṇasatte evañhi tesaṃ yathākkamaṃ sañcaraṇakasannisinnakajanopamatā upapannā hotīti ti ettha pana vuttappakārānaṃ sabbesampi sattānaṃ aniyamato gahaṇaṃ veditabbaṃ
nanu cāyaṃ dibbacakkhukathā atha kasmā tīsu bhavesūti catuvokārabhavassāpi saṅgaho kato na hi so arūpadhammārammaṇoti anuyogaṃ pariharanto tiādimāha tattha nti tīsu bhavesu nibbattasattānanti idaṃ vacananti (dī ni ṭī 1247) ayamettha ācariyassa mati evaṃ sati aṭṭhakathācariyehi aṭṭhakathāyameva yathāvutto anuyogo pariharitoti ayaṃ panettha amhākaṃ khanti  nanu cāyaṃ dibbacakkhukathā atha kasmā dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena satte passati cavamāne upapajjamānetiādinā avisesato catuvokārabhavūpagassāpi saṅgaho kato na hi  so arūpadhammārammaṇoti anuyogaṃ pariharanto tiādimāha tattha nti satte passati cavamāne upapajjamānetiādivacanaṃ evañhi sati aṭṭhakathācariyehi pāḷiyameva yathāvutto anuyogo pariharitoti yadaggena so pāḷiyaṃ pariharito tadaggena aṭṭhakathāyampi tassā atthavaṇṇanābhāvato ti kevalaṃ desanāsukhatthaṃ eva avisesena vuttaṃ na pana catuvokārabhavūpagānaṃ dibbacakkhussa āvibhāvasabbhāvato ṭhapetvā arūpabhavanti vā dvīsu bhavesūti vā satte passati kāmāvacarabhavato rūpāvacarabhavato ca cavamāneti vā kāmāvacarabhave rūpāvacarabhave ca upapajjamāneti vā vuccamānā hi desanā yathārahaṃ bhedyabhedakādivibhāvanena sukhāsukhāvabodhā ca na hoti avisesena pana evameva vuccamānā sukhāsukhāvabodhā ca desetuṃ avabodhetuñca sukaratāpayojanañhi desanāsukhatthanti vuttaṃ kasmāti āha ti dibbacakkhugocarabhūtānaṃ rūpadhammānamabhāvatoti vuttaṃ hoti

 na lokiyābhiññāsu viya abhiññāpādakaṃ nti ca vipassanāya padaṭṭhānabhūtaṃ vipassanā ca nāmesā tividhā vipassakapuggalabhedena mahābodhisattānaṃ vipassanā paccekabodhisattānaṃ vipassanā sāvakānaṃ vipassanā cāti tattha mahābodhisattānaṃ paccekabodhisattānañca vipassanā cintāmayañāṇasambandhikā sayambhuñāṇabhūtā sāvakānaṃ pana sutamayañāṇasambandhikā paropadesasambhūtā sā ṭhapetvā nevasaññānāsaññāyatanaṃ avasesarūpārūpajjhānānaṃ aññatarato vuṭṭhāyātiādinā anekadhā arūpamukhavasena catudhātuvavatthāne vuttānaṃ tesaṃ tesaṃ dhātupariggahamukhānañca aññataramukhavasena anekadhā ca  (visuddhi 2664) nānānayato vibhāvitā mahābodhisattānaṃ pana catuvīsatikoṭisatasahassamukhena pabhedagamanato nānānayaṃ sabbaññutaññāṇasannissayassa ariyamaggañāṇassa adhiṭṭhānabhūtaṃ pubbabhāgañāṇagabbhaṃ gaṇhāpentaṃ  paripākaṃ gacchantaṃ paramagambhīraṃ saṇhasukhumataraṃ anaññasādhāraṇaṃ vipassanāñāṇaṃ hoti  yaṃ aṭṭhakathāsu mahāvajirañāṇanti vuccati yassa ca pavattivibhāgena catuvīsatikoṭisatasahassappabhedassa pādakabhāvena samāpajjiyamānā catuvīsatikoṭisatasahassasaṅkhyā devasikaṃ satthu vaḷañjanasamāpattiyo vuccanti svāyaṃ buddhānaṃ vipassanācāro  (visuddhi ṭī 1144) uddesato ācariyena dassito tato so atthikehi gahetabbo idha pana sāvakānaṃ vipassanāva adhippetā
ti idaṃ kiriyāpayojanabhūte tadatthe sampadānavacanaṃ tasmā asatipi payojanavācake payojanavaseneva attho veditabboti āha ti evamīdisesu nibbānaṃ arahattamaggo ca ukkaṭṭhaniddesena idha  nāma tattha ñāṇaṃ  tassa nibbattanasaṅkhāto attho payojanaṃ tadatthāyāti attho khepeti pāpadhamme samucchindatīti  maggo so pana pāpakkhayo āsavakkhayena vinā natthi tasmā khaye ñāṇanti (dha sa suttantadukamātikā 148) ettha khayaggahaṇena āsavakkhayova vuttoti dasseti ti iminā nti āsavānamanuppādabhūte ariyaphale ñāṇaṃ khīyiṃsu āsavā etthāti  phalaṃ samitapāpatāya  samitapāpatā ca nippariyāyato arahattaphalenevāti āha nti ti ca khīṇattāti attho khīyanti āsavā etthāti  nibbānaṃ āsavakkhayāti pana samāsavasena dvibhāvaṃ katvā vuttattā āsavānaṃ khayoti padassa atthuddhāre āsavakkhayapadaggahaṇaṃ
tiādigāthā dhammapade (dha pa 253) tattha ti garahasaññino ti dūrā arā siṅghāmi vārijantiādīsu (saṃ ni 1234 jā 16116) viya hi dūratthoyaṃ nipāto ārātipi pāṭho arāsaddo viya ārāsaddopi dūratthe eko nipātoti veditabbo tadeva hi padaṃ saddasatthe udāhaṭaṃ kāmañca  arahattamaggasaṅkhātā ārā dūraṃ gatova hotīti (dha pa aṭṭha 2253) vuttaṃ tathāpi āsavavaḍḍhiyā saṅkhāre vaḍḍhento  visaṅkhārato suvidūradūro tasmā ārā so āsavakkhayāti ettha āsavakkhayapadaṃ visaṅkhārādhivacanampi sambhavatīti āha nti khayanaṃ  āsavānaṃ khaṇanirodho sesaṃ tassa pariyāyavacanaṃ bhaṅgo āsavānaṃ khayoti vuttoti yojanā idha pana nibbānampi maggopi avinābhāvato na hi nibbānamanārabbha maggeneva āsavānaṃ khayo hotīti
nti  tasmiṃ āsavānaṃ khayañāṇe ninnaṃ sesaṃ tasseva vevacanaṃ pāḷiyaṃ nti dukkhassa ariyasaccassa paricchinditvā anavasesetvā ca tadā tassa bhikkhuno paccakkhato gahitabhāvadassananti dassetuṃ ntiādi vuttaṃ tattha hi nti tassa paricchijja gahitabhāvadassanaṃ ti anavasesetvā gahitabhāvadassanaṃ tenāha ntiādi sarasalakkhaṇapaṭivedhavasena pajānanameva yathābhūtaṃ pajānanaṃ nāmāti dasseti ti iminā ti sabhāvo rasitabbo jānitabboti katvā attano raso  so eva lakkhaṇaṃ tassa asammohato paṭivijjhanenāti attho asammohato paṭivijjhanañca nāma yathā tasmiṃ ñāṇe pavatte pacchā dukkhasaccassa sarūpādiparicchede sammoho na hoti tathā tassa pavattiyeva tena vuttaṃ ti nti iminā dukkhaṃ samudeti etasmāti ti nibbacanaṃ dasseti nti dukkhaṃ dukkhasamudayo ca ti yaṃ nibbānaṃ maggassa ārammaṇapaccayaṭṭhena kāraṇabhūtaṃ āgamma nti hi kāraṇaṃ vuccati tiṭṭhati ettha phalaṃ tadāyattatāyāti katvā ti ca tadubhayavato puggalassa tadubhayassa patti viya vuttā puggalasseva hi ārammaṇakaraṇavasena nibbānappatti na tadubhayassa apica ti pāpuṇanahetu puggalassa ārammaṇakaraṇavasena samāpajjanatoti attho asamānakattuke viya hi samānakattukepi tvāpaccayassa hetvatthe pavatti saddasatthesu pākaṭā ti appavattinimittaṃ na pavattati tadubhayametenāti katvā appavattiṭṭhānaṃ vā na pavattati tadubhayametthāti katvā anena ca dukkhaṃ nirujjhati ettha etenāti vā ti nibbacanaṃ dasseti dukkhasamudayassa pana gahaṇaṃ taṃnibbattakassa nirujjhanato tassāpi nirujjhanadassanatthanti daṭṭhabbaṃ nibbānapadeyeva  ta-saddo nivattatīti ayaṃ-saddo puna vutto sabbanāmikañhi padaṃ vuttassa vā liṅgassa gāhakaṃ vuccamānassa vā ti dukkhanirodhassa nti sacchikaraṇavasena sammadeva pāpakaṃ etena ca dukkhanirodhaṃ gamayati gacchati vā etāyāti  sāyeva paṭipadā ti nibbacanaṃ dasseti
ti āsavasaṅkhātakilesavasena tadeva āsavapariyāyena dassento puna āha tasmā na ettha punaruttidosoti adhippāyo pariyāyadesanābhāvo nāma hi āveṇiko buddhadhammoti heṭṭhā vuttovāyamattho nanu ca āsavānaṃ dukkhasaccapariyāyova atthi na sesasaccapariyāyo atha kasmā sarūpato dassitasaccāniyeva kilesavasena pariyāyato puna dassento evamāhāti vuttanti saccaṃ taṃsambandhattā pana sesasaccānaṃ taṃsamudayādipariyāyopi labbhatīti  katvā evaṃ vuttanti veditabbaṃ dukkhasaccapariyāyabhūtaāsavasambandhāni hi āsavasamudayādīnīti saccāni dassentotipi yojetabbaṃ āsavānaṃ khayañāṇāyāti āraddhattā cettha āsavānameva gahaṇaṃ na sesakilesānaṃ tathā anāraddhattāti daṭṭhabbaṃ tathā hi kāmāsavāpi cittaṃ vimuccatītiādinā (dī ni 1248 ma ni 1433 319) āsavavimuttasīseneva sabbakilesavimutti vuttā idaṃ dukkhanti yathābhūtaṃ pajānātītiādinā missakamaggova idha kathito lokiyavipassanāya lokuttaramaggassa missakattāti vuttaṃ ti jānato passatoti iminā tayopi pariññāsacchikiriyābhāvanābhisamayā vuttā catusaccapajānanāya eva catukiccasiddhito pahānābhisamayo pana pārisesato vimuccatīti iminā vuttoti āha ti cattāri hi kiccāni catusaccapajānanāya eva siddhāni yathāha taṃ kho panidaṃ dukkhaṃ ariyasaccaṃ pariññātanti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhuṃ udapādītiādi (saṃ ni 51081 mahāva 15 paṭi ma 229) ayaṃ muttako nayo  ti ca hetuniddeso jānanahetu passanahetu kāmāsavāpi cittaṃ vimuccatītiādinā yojanā kāmañcettha jānanapassanakiriyānaṃ vimuccanakiriyāya ca samānakālatā tathāpi  dhammānaṃ samānakālikānampi paccayapaccayuppannatā sahajātādikoṭiyā labbhatīti hetugabbhavisesanatādassanametantipi vadanti
bhavāsavaggahaṇena cettha bhavarāgassa viya bhavadiṭṭhiyāpi samavarodhoti diṭṭhāsavassāpi saṅgaho daṭṭhabbo adhunā pana diṭṭhāsavāpi cittaṃ vimuccatīti katthaci pāṭho dissati so na porāṇo pacchā pamādalikhitoti veditabbo dīsu (ma ni aṭṭha 154) anekāsupi tatheva saṃvaṇṇitattā ettha ca kiñcāpi pāḷiyaṃ saccapaṭivedho aniyamitapuggalassa aniyamitakālavasena vutto tathāpi abhisamayakāle tassa paccuppannataṃ upādāya evaṃ jānato evaṃ passatoti vattamānakālaniddeso kato so ca kāmaṃ kassaci maggakkhaṇato paraṃ yāvajjatanā atītakāliko eva sabbapaṭhamaṃ panassa atītakālikattaṃ phalakkhaṇena veditabbanti āha nti nti phalapaccavekkhaṇañāṇaṃ tathā ceva vuttattā taggahaṇena pana tadavinābhāvato sesāni niravasesāni gahetabbāni ekadesāni vā aparipuṇṇāyapi paccavekkhaṇāya sambhavato tiādīhi padehi nāparaṃ itthattāyāti padapariyosānehi ti paccavekkhaṇañāṇassa nti pavattiṭṭhānaṃ nanu ca vimuttasmiṃ vimuttanti vuttaṃ phalameva tassa ārammaṇasaṅkhātā bhūmi atha kathaṃ khīṇā jātītiādīhi tassa bhūmidassananti codanaṃ  sodhetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ yasmā pana pahīnakilesapaccavekkhaṇena vijjamānassāpi kammassa āyatiṃ appaṭisandhikabhāvato khīṇā jātīti pajānāti yasmā ca maggapaccavekkhaṇādīhi vusitaṃ brahmacariyantiādīni pajānāti tasmā khīṇā jātītiādīhi tassa bhūmidassananti vuttaṃ hoti tena ñāṇenāti hi yathārutato avinābhāvato ca gahitena pañcavidhena paccavekkhaṇañāṇenāti attho
khīṇā jātīti ettha sotujanānaṃ suviññāpanatthaṃ parammukhā viya codanaṃ samuṭṭhāpeti tiādinā yena panādhippāyena codanā katā tadadhippāyaṃ pakāsetvā parihāraṃ vattukāmo tiādimāha na tāva vijjamānattāti vakkhamānameva hi atthaṃ manasi katvā ayaṃ codanā samuṭṭhāpitā tattha ti assa bhikkhuno atītā jāti na tāva maggabhāvanāya khīṇā tattha kāraṇamāha ti maggabhāvanāya purimatarameva nirujjhanavasena khīṇattāti adhippāyo na anāgatā assa jāti khīṇā maggabhāvanāyāti yojanā tattha kāraṇamāha ti idañca anāgatabhāvasāmaññameva gahetvā lesena codanādhippāyavibhāvanatthaṃ vadati na anāgatavisesaṃ anāgate maggabhāvanāya khepanapayogābhāvatoti attho vijjamāneyeva hi payogo sambhavati na avijjamāneti vuttaṃ hoti anāgataviseso panettha adhippeto tassa ca khepane vāyāmopi labbhateva tenāha tiādi ti ca abhāvite magge uppajjanāraho anantarajātibhedo vuccati na paccuppannā assa jāti khīṇā maggabhāvanāyāti yojanā tattha kāraṇamāha ti ekabhavapariyāpannatāya vijjamānattāti attho tattha tattha bhave paṭhamābhinibbattilakkhaṇā hi jāti yā panātiādinā pana maggabhāvanāya kilesahetuvināsanamukhena anāgatajātiyā eva khīṇabhāvo pakāsitoti daṭṭhabbaṃ ti bhavattayaggahaṇaṃ vuttanayena anavasesato jātiyā khīṇabhāvadassanatthaṃ pubbapadadvayepettha uttarapadalopo ti etthāpi eseva nayo tiādi kathañca naṃ pajānātīti codanāya sodhanāvacanaṃ tattha nti yathāvuttaṃ jātiṃ ti khīṇāsavo bhikkhu ti pajānanāya pubbabhāge pahīnakilesapaccavekkhaṇadassanaṃ evañca katvā paccavekkhaṇaparamparāya tathā pajānanā siddhāti daṭṭhabbaṃ paccavekkhaṇantaravibhāvanatthameva hi ti vattamānavacanadvayaṃ vuttaṃ jānanto hutvā jānanahetu vā pajānāti nāmāti attho
brahmacariyavāso  nāma ukkaṭṭhaniddesato maggabrahmacariyassa nibbattanamevāti āha nti samantato niravasesena vasitaṃ pariciṇṇanti attho kasmā panidaṃ so atītakālavasena pajānātīti anuyogenāha ntiādi puthujjanakalyāṇakopi hi heṭṭhā vuttalakkhaṇo sotāpattiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno  nāma dīsu (ma ni 3379) tathā eva vuttattā ti vasantā eva nāma honti na vutthavāsā ti vutthavāsattā nanu ca so idaṃ dukkhanti yathābhūtaṃ pajānātītiādinā pāḷiyaṃ sammādiṭṭhiyeva vuttā na sammāsaṅkappādayo atha kasmā nti aṭṭhaṅgikassa maggassa sādhāraṇato vuttanti sammāsaṅkappādīnampi catukiccasādhanavasena pavattito sammādiṭṭhiyā hi catūsu saccesu pariññādikiccasādhanavasena pavattamānāya sammāsaṅkappādīnampi sesānaṃ dukkhasacce pariññābhisamayānuguṇāva pavatti itarasaccesu ca nesaṃ pahānābhisamayādivasena pavatti pākaṭā evāti dukkhanirodhamaggesu yathākkamaṃ pariññāsacchikiriyābhāvanāpi yāvadeva samudayapahānatthāti katvā tadattheyeva tāsaṃ pakkhipanena kataṃ karaṇīyanti padassa adhippāyaṃ vibhāvetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ nti imināpi tadeva pakārantarena vibhāveti
kasmā panettha kataṃ karaṇīyanti atītaniddeso katoti āha tiādi ime pakārā  tabbhāvo nti dasseti ti iminā -saddo ca sampadānatthe tadatthāyāti attho te pana pakārā ariyamaggabyāpārabhūtā pariññādayo idhādhippetāti vuttaṃ ti te hi maggaṃ paccavekkhato maggānubhāvena pākaṭā hutvā upaṭṭhahanti magge paccavekkhite taṃkiccapaccavekkhaṇāyapi sukhena siddhito evaṃ sādhāraṇato catūsu maggesu paccekaṃ catukiccavasena soḷasakiccabhāvaṃ pakāsetvā tesupi kiccesu pahānameva padhānaṃ tadatthattā itaresaṃ pariññādīnanti tadeva visesato pakāsetuṃ ti āha
apica purimanayena paccavekkhaṇaparamparāya paccavekkhaṇavidhiṃ dassetvā idāni padhānattā pahīnakilesapaccavekkhaṇavidhimeva dassetuṃ evaṃ vuttantipi daṭṭhabbaṃ dutiyavikappe ayaṃ pakāro  tabbhāvo saddo cettha sampadānavacanassa kāriyabhūto nissakkattheti dasseti ti iminā imasmā evaṃ pakārāti pana vadanto pakāro nāma  pakāravantato atthato bhedo natthi yadi hi so bhedo assa tasseva so pakāro na siyā tasmā  itthaṃ-saddo pakāravantavācako atthato pana abhedepi sati avayavāvayavitādinā bhedaparikappanāvasena siyā kiñci bhedamatthaṃ tasmā itthattasaddo pakāravācakoti dasseti ayamidha  (dī ni ṭī 1248) dīsu (sārattha ṭī 114) ca āgatanayo
saddavidū pana pavattinimittānusārena evamicchanti  ayaṃ pakāro assāti  pakāravanto vicitrā hi taddhitavutti tassa bhāvo  pakāro imamatthaṃ dassento ti āhāti paṭhamavikappepi yathārahaṃ esa nayo ti sarūpakathanaṃ nti anāgataṃ ti idāni pāṭho ime pana carimakattabhāvasaṅkhātā pañcakkhandhā pariññātā tiṭṭhantīti pana dīsu (sārattha ṭī 114) idha ca  (dī ni ṭī 1248) ulliṅgitapāṭho tattha ti ekasantatipariyāpannabhāvena pacchimakattabhāvakathitā ti maggena paricchijja ñātā ti appatiṭṭhā anokāsā tiṭṭhanti etena hi tesaṃ khandhānaṃ apariññāmūlābhāvena apatiṭṭhābhāvaṃ dasseti apariññāmūlikā hi patiṭṭhā tadabhāvato pana appatiṭṭhābhāvo yathāha kabaḷīkāre ce bhikkhave āhāre atthi rāgo atthi nandī atthi taṇhā patiṭṭhitaṃ tattha viññāṇaṃ viruḷhantiādi (saṃ ni 264 kathā 296 mahāni 7) tadupamaṃ vibhāveti ti iminā yathā chinnamūlakā rukkhā mūlābhāvato appatiṭṭhā anokāsā tiṭṭhanti evametepi apariññāmūlābhāvatoti ayamettha opammasaṃsandanā ti parinibbānacittanirodhena ti anindhano nti yesu khandhesu vijjamānesu tathā tathā parikappanāsiddhā paññatti tadabhāvato tassāpi dharamānakapaññattiyā abhāvena apaññattikabhāvaṃ gamissanti paṇṇatti paññattīti hi atthato ekaṃ yathā paññāsa paṇṇāsāti paññāsa paṇṇādesoti hi akkharacintakā vadanti
 yebhuyyena  saṃkhipati saṅkucito bhavatīti  pabbatamatthakaṃ tañhi pabbatapādato anukkamena bahulaṃ saṃkhittaṃ saṅkucitaṃ hoti tenāha ti pabbatasikhareti attho ayaṃ muttako nayo  saṅkhipīyati pabbatabhāvena gaṇīyatīti saṅkhepo pabbatapariyāpanno padeso tasmiṃ pabbatapariyāpanne padeseti atthoti ti akālusiyo sā cassa anāvilatā kaddamābhāvena hotīti āha ti sapati apadāpi  samānā gacchatīti  khuddakā sippi  kā-kārassa ya-kāraṃ katvā yo muttikotipi vuccati savati pasavatīti  yaṃ jalasutti saṅkhalikāti ca voharanti samāhāre yebhuyyato napuṃsakapayogoti vuttaṃ nti evamīdisesu ti muṭṭhippamāṇā pāsāṇā ti kapālakhaṇḍāni samūhavācakassa ghaṭāsaddassa itthi liṅgassāpi dissanato gumbanti padassatthaṃ dasseti ti iminā
kāmañca sippiyasambukampi sakkharakathalampi macchagumbampi tiṭṭhantampi carantampīti ettha sakkharakathalaṃ tiṭṭhatiyeva sippiyasambukamacchagumbāni carantipi tiṭṭhantipi tathāpi sahacaraṇanayena sabbāneva caranti viya evaṃ vuttanti atthaṃ dassento tiādimāha tattha hi tiādinā yathāsambhavamatthaṃ dasseti tiādinā pana sahacaraṇanayaṃ -saddo arucisaṃsūcane tathāpīti attho ti bahūnaṃ gāvīnamantarantarā ṭhitāsu gāvīsu vijjamānāsupi ti gāviyo ti ṭhitāpi nisinnāpi  sahacaraṇanayena tiādīsu ayamadhippāyo  sippiyasambukamacchagumbānaṃ caraṇakiriyāyapi yogato ṭhānakiriyāya anekantattā ekantato tiṭṭhantameva na kadācipi carantaṃ sakkharakathalaṃ upādāya sippiyasambukampi macchagumbampi tiṭṭhantanti vuttaṃ na tu tesaṃ ṭhānakiriyamupādāya tesaṃ pana caraṇakiriyamupādāya carantampīti pi-saddalopo hettha daṭṭhabbo nti sippiyasambukamacchagumbaṃ padavasena evaṃ vuttaṃ nti sippiyasambukamacchagumbameva nti etthāpi tesaṃ ṭhānakiriyamupādāya tiṭṭhantampīti pi-saddalopo evamettha aṭṭhakathācariyehi sahacaraṇanayo dassito ācariyadhammapālattherena pana yathālābhanayopi tathā  hi vuttaṃ kiṃ vā imāya sahacariyāya yathālābhaggahaṇaṃ panettha daṭṭhabbaṃ sakkharakathalassa hi vasena tiṭṭhantanti sippisambukassa macchagumbassa ca vasena tiṭṭhantampi carantampīti evaṃ yojanā kātabbāti (dī ni ṭī 1249) alabbhamānassāpi atthassa sahayogīvasena desanāmattaṃ pati sahacaraṇanayo sādhāraṇato desitassāpi atthassa sambhavavasena vivecanaṃ pati yathālābhanayoti ubhayathāpi yujjati
evampettha vadanti   sakkharakathalaṃ tiṭṭhatiyeva itarāni carantipi tiṭṭhantipīti iminā yathālābhanayo dassito yathāsambhavaṃ atthassa vivecitattā yathā panātiādinā pana sahacaraṇanayo alabbhamānassāpi atthassa sahayogīvasena desanāmattassa vibhāvitattāti  tadetampi anupavajjameva atthassa yuttattā ñca tathā dassanassāpi sambhavatoti daṭṭhabbaṃ tiādi upamāsaṃsandanaṃ ti udakarahadassa tīre  ca nāma katthaci samuddopi vuccati rahadopi tattha gambhīro samuddo saritodakotiādīsu (dī ni 3278) katthaci jalāsayopi rahadopi tattha dharaṇī nāma yato meghā pavassanti vassā yato patāyantītiādīsu (dī ni 3281) idhāpi jalāsayoyeva so hi udakavasena raho cakkhurahādikaṃ dadātīti  o-kārassa a-kāraṃ katvā saddavidū pana udakaṃ haratīti  niruttinayenāti vadanti
tiādinā catutthajjhānāntaraṃ dassitavipassanāñāṇato paṭṭhāya yathāvuttatthassa sampiṇḍanaṃ tattha ti puna caparaṃ mahārāja bhikkhu evaṃ samāhite citte ñāṇadassanāya cittaṃ abhinīharatītiādinā ettakena etaparimāṇavantena vā vacanakkamena nti ñāṇadassananāmena dassitaṃ vipassanāñāṇaṃ tassa ca visuṃ gaṇanadassanena heṭṭhā catutthajjhānānantaraṃ vattabbatākāraṇesu tīsu nayesu tatiyanayasseva yuttatarabhāvopi dīpitoti daṭṭhabbaṃ manomayañāṇassa iddhividhasamavarodhitabhāve  (visuddhi 2379 ādayo) vuttepi idha pāḷiyaṃ visuṃ desitattā visuṃ eva gahaṇaṃ tathā desanā ca pāṭiyekkasandiṭṭhikasāmaññaphalatthāti daṭṭhabbaṃ anāgataṃsañāṇayathākammūpagañāṇadvayassa  pāḷiyaṃ anāgatattā nti vuttaṃ tabbasena nipphannattā taggahaṇeneva gahitaṃ taṃ ñāṇadvayanti vuttaṃ hoti dibbacakkhussa hi anāgataṃsañāṇaṃ yathākammūpagañāṇañcāti dvepi ñāṇāni paribhaṇḍāni hontīti nti cutūpapātañāṇanāmena dassitaṃ dibbacakkhuñāṇaṃ
sabbesaṃ pana dasannaṃ ñāṇānaṃ ārammaṇavibhāgassa  anāgatattā tatthānāgatañāṇānaṃ ārammaṇavibhāgaṃ dassetuṃ ntiādi vuttaṃ nti dasannaṃ ñāṇānaṃ ti tasmiṃ ārammaṇavibhāge tesu vā dasasu ñāṇesu bhūmibhedato parittamahaggataṃ kālabhedato atītānāgatapaccuppannaṃ santānabhedato ajjhattabahiddhā cāti  parittārammaṇāditikattayeneva hi tassa ārammaṇavibhāgo na maggārammaṇatikena ti attanā nimmitaṃ rūpārammaṇameva attanā vā nimmite manomaye kāye vijjamānaṃ rūpāyatanamevātipi yujjati idañhi tassa ñāṇassa abhinimmiyamāne manomaye kāye rūpāyatanamevārabbha pavattanato vuttaṃ na pana tattha gandhāyatanādīnamabhāvato  na hi rūpakalāpo gandhāyatanādivirahito atthīti sabbathā parinipphannameva nimmitarūpaṃ tenāha nti yathākkamaṃ bhūmikālasantānabhedato tibbidhārammaṇanti attho nibbānavasena ekadhammārammaṇampi samānaṃ āsavakkhayañāṇaṃ parittārammaṇāditikavasena tividhārammaṇaṃ dassetuṃ nti vuttaṃ tañhi parittatikavasena appamāṇārammaṇaṃ ajjhattikavasena bahiddhārammaṇaṃ atītatikavasena navattabbārammaṇañca hoti
uttaritarasaddo paṇītatarasaddo ca pariyāyoti dasseti nti iminā ratanakūṭaṃ viya kūṭāgārassa arahattaṃ kūṭaṃ uttamaṅgabhūtaṃ bhagavato desanāya arahattapariyosānattāti āha ti ti titthakaramataharavibhāviniṃ nānāvidhakuhanalapanādimicchājīvaviddhaṃsiniṃ tividhasīlālaṅkataparamasallekhapaṭipattiparidīpiniṃ jhānābhiññādiuttarimanussadhammavibhūsiniṃ cuddasavidhamahāsāmaññphalapaṭimaṇḍitaṃ anaññasādhāraṇaṃ sāmaññaphaladesanaṃ ratanāgāraṃ  viya ratanakūṭena arahattakūṭena niṭṭhāpesi vimuttasminti iminā arahattaphalassa desitattāti attho

 ettāvatā bhagavatā desitassa sāmaññaphalasuttassa atthavaṇṇanaṃ katvā idāni dhammasaṅgāhakehi saṅgītassa evaṃ vuttetiādipāṭhassapi atthavaṇṇanaṃ karonto paṭhamaṃ sambandhaṃ dassetuṃ tiādimāha ti tasmiṃ tasmiṃ sāmaññaphale suttapadese vā karaṇaṃ  sādhu iti kāro tathā sādhu bhagavā sādhu sugatātiādinā taṃ pavattento nti desanāya ādiñca majjhañca pariyosānañca  sādaraṃ gāravaṃ  cintetvāti ettha idaṃ pubbakālakiriyāvacanaṃ ime pañhe puthū samaṇabrāhmaṇe pucchanto ahaṃ ciraṃ vata amhi evaṃ pucchantopi ahaṃ thuse koṭṭento viya kañci sāraṃ nālatthanti yojanā tathā yo vissajjesi tassa bhagavato guṇasampadā aho vata dasabalassa guṇānubhāvaṃ ajānanto ahaṃ vañcito suciraṃ vata amhīti ti ca aññāṇena vañcito āvaṭṭito mohena paṭicchādito amhīti vuttaṃ hoti tenāha ti sāmaññajotanā hi visese avatiṭṭhati cintetvā āvikarontoti sambandho ullaṅghanasamatthāyapi ubbegapītiyā anullaṅghanampi siyāti āha ti ti ca phusitasarīroti attho na byāpitasarīroti  sabbāya pītiyā abyāpitattā nti attano pasādassa āvikaraṇaṃ upāsakattapavedanañca  dhammasaṅgāhakehi
ti atikkantā vigatā vigatabhāvo ca khayo evāti āha ti tathā hi vuttaṃ ti ti ativiya kantataro manoramo tādiso ca sundaro bhaddako nāmāti vuttaṃ ti
tiādi gāthā  (vi va 857) tattha ti devanāgayakkhagandhabbādīsu katamo ti mama ti pāde liṅgavipariyāyoyaṃ ti īdisāya deviddhiyā ti īdisena parivārena parijanena  ca nti jalanto vijjotamāno ti ativiya kantena kamanīyena abhirūpenāti vuttaṃ hoti ti chavivaṇṇena sarīravaṇṇanibhāya ti sabbā dasapi disā obhāsayanto cando viya sūriyo viya ca ekobhāsaṃ ekālokaṃ karonto ko vandatīti sambandho
ti atirekarūpe uḷāravaṇṇena sampannarūpe ti abhianumodane abhippamoditabhāve kimatthiyaṃ abbhānumodaneti vacananti āha tiādi yuttaṃ tāva hotu abbhānumodane kasmā panāyaṃ dvikkhattuṃ vuttoti codanāya sodhanāmukhena āmeḍitavisayaṃ niddhāreti tiādinā iminā saddalakkhaṇena hetubhūtena evaṃ vutto iminā ca iminā ca visayenāti vuttaṃ hoti sādhu sādhu bhanteti āmeḍitavasena atthaṃ dassetvā tassa visayaṃ niddhārento evamāhātipi sambandhaṃ vadanti tattha coro coro sappo sappotiādīsu  vijjha vijjha pahara paharātiādīsu  sādhu sādhūtiādīsu (saṃ ni 2127 335 51085)  gaccha gaccha lunāhi lunāhītiādīsu  āgaccha āgacchātiādīsu  buddho buddhoti cintentotiādīsu (bu vaṃ 244)  abhikkamathāyasmanto abhikkamathāyasmantotiādīsu (dī ni 320 a ni 911)  kahaṃ ekaputtaka kahaṃ ekaputtakātiādīsu (saṃ ni 263)  aho sukhaṃ aho sukhantiādīsu (udā 20 dī ni 3305) saddo avuttasamuccayattho tena garahā asammānādīnaṃ saṅgaho daṭṭhabbo pāpo pāpotiādīsu hi  abhirūpaka abhirūpakātiādīsu  evametesu navasu aññesu ca visayesu āmeḍitavacanaṃ  budho kareyya yojeyyāti attho āmeḍanaṃ punappunamuccāraṇaṃ āmeḍīyati vā punappunamuccārīyatīti  ekassevatthassa dvattikkhattuṃ vacanaṃ saddo hi ummādane āpubbo tu dvattikkhattumuccāraṇe vattati yathā etadeva yadā vākya-māmeḍayati vāsavoti
evaṃ  āmeḍitavasena dvikkhattuṃ vuttabhāvaṃ dassetvā idāni nayidaṃ āmeḍitavaseneva dvikkhattuṃ vuttaṃ atha kho paccekamatthadvayavasenapīti dassento tiādimāha āmeḍitavasena atthaṃ dassetvā vicchāvasenāpi dassento evamāhātipi vadanti tadayuttameva byāpetabbassa dvikkhattumavuttattā byāpetabbassa hi byāpakena guṇakiriyādabbena byāpanicchāya dvattikkhattuṃ vacanaṃ vicchā yathā gāmo gāmo ramaṇīyoti tattha nti abhikkamanīyaṃ tabbhāvo ca atiiṭṭhatāyāti vuttaṃ ntiādi padattayañcetaṃ pariyāyavacanaṃ ti dvīsu abhikkantasaddesu abhikkantanti vacanaṃ apekkhitvā napuṃsakaliṅgena vuttaṃ taṃ pana bhagavato vacanaṃ dhammadesanāyevāti katvā ti āha yāyaṃ bhagavato dhammadesanā mayā sutā tadidaṃ bhagavato dhammadesanāsaṅkhātaṃ vacanaṃ abhikkantanti attho evaṃ paṭiniddesopi hi atthato abhedattā yutto eva yattha ca dinnaṃ mahapphalamāhūtiādīsu (vi va 888) viya abhikkantanti vuttassa vā atthamattadassanaṃ etaṃ tasmā atthavasena liṅgavibhattivipariṇāmo veditabbo kāriyavipariṇāmavasena cettha vibhattivipariṇāmatā vacananti hettha seso abhikkantaṃ bhagavato vacanaṃ yāyaṃ bhagavato dhammadesanā mayā sutā sā abhikkantaṃ abhikkantāti attho dutiyapadepi abhikkantanti pasādanaṃ apekkhitvā napuṃsakaliṅgena vuttantiādinā yathārahamesa nayo netabbo
ntiādinā atthadvayasarūpaṃ dasseti tattha ti rāgādikilesadosaviddhaṃsanato ti sīlādiguṇānaṃ sampādanavasena adhigamāpanato ye guṇe desanā adhigameti tesu guṇādhigamanatoti vuttesuyeva guṇesu padhānabhūtā guṇā dassetabbāti te padhānabhūte guṇe tāva dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ saddhāpadhānā hi lokiyā guṇā paññāpadhānā lokuttarāti padhānaniddeso cesa desanāya adhigametabbehi sīlasamādhidukādīhipi yojanāsambhavato aññampi atthadvayaṃ dasseti tiādinā sīlādiatthasampattiyā  sabhāvaniruttisampattiyā  suviññeyyasaddapayogatāya  saṇhasukhumabhāvena dubbiññeyyatthatāya  siniddhamudumadhurasaddapayogatāya  vipulavisuddhapemanīyatthatāya  mānātimānavidhamanena  thambhasārambhanimmaddanena  hitādhippāyappavattiyā paresaṃ rāgapariḷāhādivūpasamanena  kilesandhakāravidhamanena  avadātaṃ odātanti ca atthato ekaṃ karavīkarutamañjutāya  pubbāparāviruddhasuvisuddhatāya  āpātharamaṇīyatāya eva  vimaddakkhamatāya hitajjhāsayappavattitāya ca ti evamettha attho veditabbo saddena pana saṃsāracakkanivattanato saddhammacakkappavattanato micchāvādaviddhaṃsanato sammāvādapatiṭṭhāpanato akusalamūlasamuddharaṇato kusalamūlasaṃropanato apāyadvāravidhānato saggamaggadvāravivaraṇato pariyuṭṭhānavūpasamanato anusayasamugghāṭanatoti evamādīnaṃ saṅgaho daṭṭhabbo
